40N||18||7||Kwo kwansukumuk shotI kik, osam ni nshke'ntuwunIn iw sI ke'nomkuk e'wipiamkuk nshke'ntuwunIn kokwansukumuk cI onInIpie'tot i nshke'ntuwun.
40N||18||8||KishpIn iknIc, tanake' i ksIt, ocImiashtotmIn kishkshIn, ipi nkoci pukiton, wusimI wunIt, kin pitike'n pmatsiwunuk knIce'n, ipi ksIte'n pnacak, icI i e'wi in nish knIce'n tanake' ksIte'n, icI e'wipuke'nukon kakuk shkote'k.
40N||18||9||KishpIn ke'ikshkishuk ocImiashtotmIn kcIpiton nkoci pukiton; wusimI owunIt kin pitike'n shi pmatsowunuk; mtIno nkotuk kshkishuk, icI e'wi-ion nish kshkishkwe'n e'wipukicikasiIn namkumuk shkote'k.
40N||18||10||Akwamsuk e'wipwa ianwe'nme'k otI nkot e'kaciIt, OtI ktInum, IpI shpumuk mishInwe'mwan pIne'’ wapmawan shiw oshkishkonuk ni NosIn e'ciIt shpumuk kishkok.
40N||18||11||O We'kwIsmukot NInwun kipie' e'wike'skonat ni kakiwanincIn,
40N||18||12||TInicI e'shte'aie'k? KishpIn nInI iuwat nkotwak mantanshIn, icI nkot kiwaninIt, conI onukinasin ni shak tso mtInIshIshaka, icI e'shiat shi e'pmIkwtakiw onunuk, icI e'pantawapmat ni kakiwanincIn.
40N||18||13||KishpIn cI mkuwat, we'we'nI ktInum, wusimI su mciwe'nmo ni nkot mantanshIn, icI ni shaktso mtInI shI shaka; kapwakiwanincIn.
40N||18||14||Iw sI nasap; cowin otIne'nmasin; Koswa e'iIt shpumuk, notI nkot e'kacinIncIn e'wipnatsInut.
40N||18||15||MinI kishpIn kikane' mIcitotakwiIn, shian, ipi witmo iw omIcshowe'psowun te'pnak kin, ipi win, nshukI kishpIn cI psItakwiIn; kikshkaase' kikane'.
40N||18||16||KishpIn kI pwapsItakwiIn moice'o nkot tanake', nish, wusimI, icI winwa otukitowunawa ki nish, tanake' nswI, ke'ocI wishkIsuk i kitukitonuwan.
40N||18||17||KishpIn cI ni pwaopsItwat witmoki e'cmaacIk, kishpIn cI pwapsItwat ni anmue'ancIn, ne'num ke'cwa me'mataosIt, ipi maocIcke' onInI.
40N||18||18||We'we'nI ktInum, We'kwe'ntuk ke'tkoptoie'k shotI kik, shi ke'tkopte' shpumuk, ipi we'kwe'ntuk ke'iapskonme'k shotI kik, ke'iapskonkate' shi shpumuk.
40N||18||19||MinI otI ktInum; KishpIn nish kinwa ie'ne'ntume'k shotI kik tshItme'ke'ko; winwa ntotmowat iw ke'nomkItnuk Nos e'iIt, shpumuk kishkok.
40N||18||20||KishpIn nish, tanake' nswI, ocI maoce'tiwat nin tnoswunuk shiw nkIiI nawi iukwan e'ciiuwat.
40N||18||21||IcI Pitu okipie'naskawan, otI cI okinan, Te'pe'nmin, TInicItsuk nikane' miashtotwut icI nin, e'wipone'nmuk? nashnI nouksuk?
40N||18||22||Cisus cI otI okinan, otIsI cokite'nse'non nash nouktsuk, otIsI nush nouktsomtInI tsuk nouk.
40N||18||23||OtIsI she'nakwIt okumauwun shpumuk ke'cwa kcI-okuma, ne'twe'nmat opmitakaimIn e'witpukot.
40N||18||24||Pic cI wawe'pktasot, nkot kipie'twa mtatsuk mtatswak kcIshoniaiIn me'snamakot.
40N||18||25||CocI ke'ko okiiIsin e'witpuwe'k, Te'pe'nmukwocIn, kishawe' win e'witawe'k ipi niwiwun, ipi onicanse'iIn, ipi caye'k ka‘tot icI e'witpukate'nuk iw, omIsInukIn.
40N||18||26||NicI pmitakaimIn okiowucikwnItakon, otI cI okinan, Te'pe'nmin nocma pwishIn, icI caye'k kIshtpuon.
40N||18||27||NicI te'pe'nmukwocIn, okishuwe'nmukon, ipi okipkItnukon, icI e'kiwe'pne'makot i me'snamowat.
40N||18||28||IcI o pmtaka e'kisakuk, icI nkot e'kimkawat wic pmitakaiIn kamsInamakot, nkotwak shomanke'In, icI e'kimackonat, e'ki kpe'ne'we'nat; otI cI okinan, tpuoshIn me'snumoiIn.
40N||18||29||IcI ni wic pmitakaiIn kipukson osItik, e'kimatmat; otI cI okinan, PwishIn icI caye'k ke'cI tpu‘onan.
40N||18||30||Cocu papIsh, ikiwupitke'we'pnan shi kpakwotiwkomkok, i e'witpu ukot i me'sna‘makot.
40N||18||31||Pic cI ni wic pmitakaiIn kawaptumwat e'totwumIt cicIkisate'ntumwuk, icI e'kinaskawawat, ipi okiwit mowawan, ni te'pe'nmukwacIn caye'k katotwumIt,
40N||18||32||IcI ni te'pe'nmukwcIn kakishntomkot otI okinan, O! ke'kie'patsin pmitaka kipone'ntumon caye'k me'snamoiIn, osam i kishIntawe'num,
40N||18||33||ConukwnI ke'kin i ktakishIshuwe'nmasi, o kicpmitaka. nin kashIshuwe'nme'nan.
40N||18||34||IcI ni te'pe'nmukwcIn kin shkatsin, ipi okipkItnumwan, ni ke'tmakawe'ncIn, pama kitpu‘uk caye'k i kamsInamakwcIn.
40N||18||35||Iwsuke' win nasap shpumuk Nos, ke'totakwie'k, kishpIn kte'iwak pwapone'ntumwe'k cak kikane'iwa me'ctotakwie'k.
40N||19||1||Iw kashowe'puk pic Cisus kakishkitot, shi kiwcImaci Ke'ne'niuk, icI e'kishiat e'kokmukwe'anak Cwtie'uk e'shwIiokwan Catanuk.
40N||19||2||Kicmaoce'tincIn cI okpmInashkakon; shiwcI okine'se'an.
40N||19||3||KicI kI Pe'nisiuk kipie'naskakon, e'wikwcI te'pe'nmawat, otI cI okinawan; Ta‘wunItnI nInI we'pinat wiwun cak ke'ko?
40N||19||4||Okinkwe'twe'ncI, otI okinan, conu wikakwaptusinawa, mIsInukInuk win kaoshaat ne'tum okiwshuan nInIwun ipi kwe'n.
40N||19||5||OtI kakItot iw ie'i nInI ke'ocI nkInat, osun ipi okie'iIn; icI ke'cI iuwat wiwun, ipi e'nishwawat kInkot nInI otIwiasmawa.
40N||19||6||IwcI ie'i we'cpwanishwawat, mtIno nkotnInI otI wiasmawa; IwcI Kshe'mIne'to kanishostot coin ntoac nInI okupapkie'ptosin.
40N||19||7||OtI cI okinawan, TacI Mosus kashukatokie't e'wiminkIt we'npie'kate'k msInukIn icI e'wiwe'pnukIt.
40N||19||8||OtI cI okinan, E'iwishkiaksIni kte'‘iwan, Mosus kaocI ne'nmukwie'k e'wiwe'pne'k kiwuwak; ke'i!aie'k coi konomkIsnon.
40N||19||9||NincI ktInum, We'kwe'ntuk ke'we'pnakwan wiwun, kishpIn pwa waonIshkawanIt okwe' ipi pe'kansIncIn wiwut waonIshkaiwI, ipi we'kwe'ntuk ke'owiwkwe'n niwe'pnukasnIt win waonIshkaiwI.
40N||19||10||E'knomowacIn otI okikon, KishpIn wIiI showe'‘psIt otI nInI ni wiwun; cota owunse'non e'wiwiwuk.
40N||19||11||OtI cI okinan, Caye'k nInwuk co otaotapnIsinawa, otI kikitowun; mtIno ki ke'mincIk.
40N||19||12||AnIt ionukuk kishI nikwuk, kashu nikukwat okie'owan, ipi anIt ionukuk kiwshiak ionukuk ni nInwun, ipi anIt ionukuk okiwshItonawa wiwuwa ionukuk, shpumukcI okumauwun, we'ctotatsowat, Win ke'kshkItot wiwtapnuk, nocma okaotapnan.
40N||19||13||IcI e'kipie'twawat akacinIncIn pInoce'iIn e'wipkItnuk, niw onIce'n wiwunuk, ipi e'winumat, icI ni ke'knomowacIn; okimiashknonawan.
40N||19||14||OtI cI Cisus kikIto, Nocma pkItnuk ki pe'piwsicuk pInoce'iuk, ipi ke'ko knumoake'kon e'wipie'naskawat, iwkshe' e'shnakwuk okumauwun shpumuk kishkok.
40N||19||15||IcI e'kipkItnuk nione'ce'n wiwunuk, kinmamacicI.
40N||19||16||PInI cI, nkot okipie'naskakon, ipi otI, okikon Manoshuwe'psin Ke'knomake'n; we'kwnicI ke'totman we'onuk e'wikshkItoian, kake'pmatsowun?
40N||19||17||IcI otI okinan, TacI we'tshInkashiIn me'noshuwe'psin? Cosuwi wIiI mnoshuwe'psusi, mtIno nkot, ocI Kshe'mIne'to: kishpIn, wiwikwcIpitike'n shi pmatsonuk nakitowe'ntum ni okukie'kwe'wunun.
40N||19||18||OtI cI okinan, TIninIncI ni? Cisus cI okikito, Ke'ko nshowe'kIn; Ke'ko, waonIshkaiwukIn, Ke'ko kmotkIn, Ke'ko wIiI knoshkacimakIn;
40N||19||19||KcIpite'num Kos ipi kie'‘, ipi Tpash kic pmatsi, e'pic tpantIsiun.
40N||19||20||OcI oshkInwe' otI okinan, Caye'ksI notI, kapie'shIcke'ian e'kopie'kishkiian, We'kwnicI nowate'shIcke'ian.
40N||19||21||Cisus cI otI okinan; KishpIn waowike'swune'n, shian, ipi tawe'n e'ton icI kuminak ke'tmakse'cuk; te'pe'nwe'osawun ke'iIn, ipI shpumuk, ipi pie'pmInashkaoshIn.
40N||19||22||NIsh cI o oshkInwe' kanotuk; i kItwun; kin mamaci kikisate'ntum, osam kikcI tpe'nwe'osI.
40N||19||23||IcI kanat Cisus ni e'knomowacIn, We'we'nI ktInum, ke'ctpe'nwe'osIt nshnI kawa okIshkiton e'wipitike't shi okumau wunuk shpumuk.
40N||19||24||MinI otI ktInum, WusimI tawe'npInsI o kcIwe'si shipanote't e'wankoianuk, shapnukIn, icI ke'ctpe'nwe'osIt nInI e'wipitike't shiw otokumauwunuk Kshe'mIne'to.
40N||19||25||IcI ni kiknomowacIn, kanotmowat kikcImamkate'ntumwuk, otI kikItwuk, We'nicI ke'ke'skwit?
40N||19||26||Cisus cI okiwapman, ipi otI okinan, NInwuk sI, co otI otakshkItosinawa, winie'k, Kshe'mIne'to cake'ko otakshkIton.
40N||19||27||IcI e'kinkwe'twat Pitu ipi otI okinan PInI ninan nkinkItamIn caye'k, icI e'kipmnashkonkon: We'knicI ke'ie'iak?
40N||19||28||Cisus cI otI okinan, We'we'nI ktInum Kinwa pie'pmnashkawie'k shi iacnikiItiwnuk, pic We'kwIsmukot NInwun kicipitupIt, shiw ome'nwankocipitupwunuk; kinwa ke' kcipitupum mtatso shIntInish cipitupwukwuk tpakwne'k ki mtatso shIntInish e'tswe'nkIswat Isniuk.
40N||19||29||E'tshuwat, ki kankItikuk e'tawacIn tanaka, wikae'iIn, tanake' omIse'iIn, tanake' osIn, tanake' okie'iIn, tanaka wiwun, tanake' onicansIn, tanaka otukim, nin ocInkItmowat, ntInoswunuk, oke'ie'nawa nkotwak tso, ipi oke'ie'nawa ke'ciiuwat kake' pmatsowunuk.
40N||19||30||NIsh cI kumane'k kie'ne'tumIscuk kiw kIshkwIshnok; ipi ki kIshkwIshkuk kne'tmIshnok.
40N||20||1||OTI sI okumauwun shpumuk e'shnakwuk ke'cwa nInI katpe'ntuk wikwam, kasakuk kukishie'p e'winokanat wamice'witakwcIn, shiw siwnokamshu ktukanuk.
40N||20||2||Pic cI kanat ni makicIwincIn, nkot shInIn e'kishkiwuk, okikatonan shi siwnokamshu ktukanuk.
40N||20||3||IcI e'kimacit cI, e'iaptu naokwe'nuk icI e'kiwapmat pakansIncIn e'nipwunIt, ke'ko e'pwamiktumnIt shiw e'tshitatuk.
40N||20||4||IcI otI okinan. Shiak ke' kinwa, shiw siwnokamshI ktukanuk, ipi we'kwe'ntuk ke'shI wunuk, i ke'shIminukon. IcI e'kimaciwat.
40N||20||5||MinI Kimaci naokwe'nuk, ipi kaiaptosanuk icI nasap kishIcke'.
40N||20||6||NkotupukIn e'pwamshu pkIshmok kishie'wak, ipi okimkawan anIt e'ni powe'nIt ke'ko e'pwamiktumnIt, icI otI okinan, We'kwnicI shotI we'cnipoie'k ne'ie'kIn ke'ko e'pwamiktme'k?
40N||20||7||OtI cI okikon, osam cowIiI nInI nokankosinan. IcI otI okinan, Shiak, ke'kinwa shi siwnokamshI ktukanuk; we'we'nIcI ke'pite'ntakwtokwe'n kuke'ie'nawa.
40N||20||8||PamacI pic, e'nmupkonianuk, te'pe'ntuk, i siwnokamshu ktukan otI okinan, ni pmitakaimIn; Ntom ki makice'wicuk mish ke'shkitowat, shkwe'iak o kapiat tpa‘o ne'tum icI o ne'tum kapiat shkwe'iak tpa‘o.
40N||20||9||Pic kapishiawat kikanokancuk nkot tpukIn e'pwamshI pkIshmok, e'tshawat kiminak nkot shInIn.
40N||20||10||Pic cI kapiIshawat ne'ptum, kanokancuk wusimI nkuminkomIn kine'ntum wuk. winwa ke' nasap kiminak e'tshawat nInI nkot shInIn.
40N||20||11||IcI kakIshminkowat, okimto‘mawan me'noshuwe'psIncIn ni nInwun, we'tu wikwamnIncIn.
40N||20||12||OtI kikItwuk, KotI shkwe'iak kimikce'wik, mtIno nkot tpukIn, icI kin kiie'i naoshiImIn ninancI, wi nkipi ke'ie'kwsImIn, shi e'wiskate'k e'kishkiwuk.
40N||20||13||Okinkwe'twancI ninkit, otI okinan, Nikan, cosuwi kimiashtotosnon, conukwI kiwnwacisi e'witponan, nkot shInIn?
40N||20||14||OtapnIn te'pe'ntumIn, ipi macin. Nkumina ote' shkwe'iak pie'mikce'wit kin kashuminan.
40N||20||15||ConI owunse'non nin e'wi totman e'shte'aian te'pe'ntuman? InI kshkishuk we'cmiashu we'psinkuk, osam nin e'mnoshuwe'pse'an?
40N||20||16||Kisu shkwe'iak kne'tmIswuk, ipi ki ne'tum shkwe'iak; anwu mce'shntomak nIshce' pke'ci we'napcIkaswuk,
40N||20||17||Cisus cI e'nmapiskat e'ishat Cinose'numuk, okimacinan ni mtatso shItnish ke'knomowacIn, icI e'nmInshIke'osawat e'nmIshiawat, otI okinan.
40N||20||18||PInI, ktIshamIn ipI Cinose'ne'muk, icI We'kwIsmukot NInwun kupkItna shi kcI me'matmocuk ipi ki we'npie'ke'ncIn, icI ke'cI pkIte'nmawat e'winsIckasnIt.
40N||20||19||OkupkItnumwawancI, ni me'mataosIncIn e'winaptotwanIt, ipi e'wipsItie'wanIt, ipi e'wiskakwukasnIt, icI nso kishkuk minI kupsukwi.
40N||20||20||IcI e'kipie'naskakot niw kie'iwan ni Se'piti nicansIn, okipie'wice'okon ni okwIsIn, e'pie' owuciwkwnItakot e'ntuwe'ntumakot ke'ko.
40N||20||21||OtI cI okinan, We'kwnicI ne'twe'ntumIn? OtI cI okinan, Ne'num, kotI nish nkwIsuk, e'wicipitupwat, nkot kte'pniwnak, ipi o nkot knumciwnak, shiw ktokumauwunuk.
40N||20||22||Cisus cI okinkwe'twan, otI kikIto, CosI kuke'ntusinawa ne'totmoie'k, KtakshkItonawanI e'wimnukwe'ie'k shi mnukwackInuk, nin watshumnukwe'ian, ipi e'wi kcitapie'nkoie'k i kcitapie'nwe'wun, e'shIkcitapie'nkoian. OtI ci okinawan ntakshkItomInsI.
40N||20||23||IcI otI okinan. We'we'nIsI kamnukwe'nawa i nmInkwackIn, ipi kukcitapie'nkom, i kcitapie'nwe'wun e'sh kcitapie'nkoian, icI ie'k e'wi cipitupie'k shi nte'pniwnak, ipi numciwnak coin nin i ntpe'ntusin e'wimikwian, kisie'k kuminak e'twaknukwacIn Nos.
40N||20||24||Pic cI ki mtatso kanotmoat, okinsItawe'nmawan, ni nish we'wikane'itIncIn.
40N||20||25||Cisus cI okintoman e'ciIt, otI kikIto, Kuke'nmawaksI ki okumak ki Me'mataose'cuk, otI tpakwnukwan; ipi cIki ke'cne'ntakwse'cuk okIcnapne'nkwan.
40N||20||26||Cocu wi kinwa a knomkIsnon; we'kwe'ntuk kinwa ke'kcine'ntakwsukwe'n, oie'o, nocma win kupmitakwa.
40N||20||27||We'kwe'ntukI kinwa ke'okumaokwe'n; nocma win kupmitakwa.
40N||20||28||Ie'inomkIt ke'cwa We'kwIsmukot NInwun e'ki pwapie' pmitwut; mtIno e'kipie' pmitake't, ipi e'wimikoe't, opmatsuwun e'witpuke't ni mane'ncIn.
40N||20||29||Pic cI e'nmumaciwat Cunikoiuk; ke'cmaoce'tincIn, okipmInashkakon,
40N||20||30||PInI, nish ke'kie' pikwancIn nInwun, e'cipitupnIt cikimie'w kanotake'wat, ni CisusIn e'pmose'nIt kinotaksik, otI kikItwuk, Shuwe'nmIshInak O Te'pe'nmiak, We'kwIsmukwiIn Te'pIt.
40N||20||31||KicI maoce'ticIk okiknuumowawan, e'wi tokmupinIt; wusimIcI kinotaksik otI kikItwuk, Shuwe'nmIshInak O Te'pe'nmiak We'kwIsmukwiIn Te'pIt.
40N||20||32||IcI Cisus tokum, e'kinipwIt, ipi okintomat, otI okinan, We'kwnicI pe'kose'nmie'k, i watotonkon?
40N||20||33||OtI cI okikon, Te'pe'nmiak, notI nshkishkonanIn e'winsakwnImIn.
40N||20||34||IcI Cisus okishuwe'nman, ipi okitaknumwan, niw shkishkonIn, icI papuk e'kintawapwat, ipi okipmInashkakon.
40N||21||1||PIC cI pe'shoc e'nme'iawat Cinose'numuk shi kapiawat Pe'pe'ciuk, shi e'pkotniak AnIpiuk, icI Cisus e'ki nokanat nish ke'knomowacIn;
40N||21||2||OtI cI okinan, Shiak sI shi otane'suk wusoci iukwan e'ie'k kie'nup cI kumkuwawa me'makshe' e'tkopsot, ipi ne'makshe'sun, e'wickapwItwat, iapskopinuk, icI ke'cI pie'twe'ie'k.
40N||21||3||KishpIn cI wIiI nInI, ke'ko koie'k; otI knawa, Te'pe'nke't onItwe'nman, icI papuk kupkIte'ntumakwa.
40N||21||4||Caye'ksI otI kitotam, e'wite'pwe'wunukuk kakitot Nakanacimot otI kItwak.
40N||21||5||Witomouk otansun, Sayan, PInI kitokumam, kupie'naskak, kacwe'nmo e'pie'tomkot me'makshe'iIn, ipi me'makshe'sIn, we'nicansumacIn me'makshe'.
40N||21||6||Kimacik cI ni ke'knomawacIn, icI kiwIshIcke'k Cisus kanat.
40N||21||7||Okipie'nawancI ni me'makshe'iIn, ipi ni me'makshe'sIn, okitonawancI paskumwacIn; icI kwuciukwan e'ki cipitupawat.
40N||21||8||Ke'cmaoce'ticuk cI, okishuwe'ksItonawan opiskumwaknawan shi mie'wuk anItkI okikishktukwne'anawan ni mtukwe'n, icI e'kipukitowat shi mie'wuk.
40N||21||9||IcI ki maoce'ticIk kanmI nikanicIk, ipi kanmupme'nashkawacuk, kinmI wishkwe'we'ksik, otI kikItwuk, Ke'skonwe'n We'kwIsmukwiIn, Te'pIt Mnawankose' o, pie'iat otunoswunuk Kshe'mIne'ton, Nocma kinwusimI ke'skonwe'n!
40N||21||10||Pic kapiat shi Cinose'numuk; caye'k shi kaicuk kcI otanuk kimacik, otI kikItwuk, We'nicI otI?
40N||21||11||KicI maoce'ticuk kikItwuk, Cisus sI otI Nakanacimot we'cpiat, Ne'se'nut iukwanuk Ke'niniuk.
40N||21||12||Cisus cI kipitike', Kshe'mIne'to okIcnume'okumkok, okisakicuwe'pnancI, caye'k e'tawe'n cIn, ipi kashpInItasnIncIn, shi kcI nume'okumkok ipi okikwe'npowe'pnanIn ni topwonIn, e'icuk iashtonkuk shonia, ipi ki otuptie'pwunwan, e'tawe'cuk, ni mIne'to mimin.
40N||21||13||OtI cI okinan, OtI kikishnupie'kate' e'taian kshInkate' e'tshu nume'okumuk; kinwa cI kmotiwkumuk kiwshItonawa.
40N||21||14||Ke'kie' pikwacuk, ipi me'akatacuk okipie'naskakon, shi kcInume'okumkok icI e'kine'se'at.
40N||21||15||IcI ki kcI-me'matmocIk, ipi we'npie'ke'cIk kawapitumwawat, i kashumataocIke'nIt, ipi pInoce'iIn; e'wIshkwe'we'ksInIt shi kcI-nume'okumkok, ipi otI e'kItwat, Ke'skonwe'n We'kwIsmukwiIn o Te'pIt; icI kikcIn shke'ntumwuk.
40N||21||16||OtI cI okikon, KnotwaknukotI e'kItowat, icI Cisus otI okinan; E'; Conu wikakwaptIsinawa e'shpie'kate'k misInukIn; Shiw otoniwak ki pInoce'ie'k, ipi nwancuk, kitockishton kwiuk winwate'ntumwun.
40N||21||17||OkinknancI, kiw cI maci shi kcIotanuk e'kishiat Pe'te'ne'iuk, icI shi e'kikIshIt.
40N||21||18||IcI e'kishie'pwunuk, ne'iap e'nmupiskat, e'shiat shi kcIotanuk kipkIte',
40N||21||19||Pic cI e'wapmat kcI siwnokamIshe'n shiw kpumie'kIn, okinaskawan, cocI ke'ko okimkusin mtIno tukupukwe'n, otI cI okishitan, Cowi ka minI kumicImosi. IcI kie'nup kcI siwnokamIsh kinpopkIso.
40N||21||20||IcI ki kiknomowacIn kawaptumwat, kimamkate'ntumwuk, otIcI kikItwuk, TInicI kie'nup otI kcI SiwnokamIsh e'sh npopkIsot.
40N||21||21||Cisus cI okinkwe'twan otI ikinan, We'we'nI ktInum, KishpIn ie'ie'k i te'pwe'we'ntumwun, ipi pwaianwe'ntusie'k, cowi otI kashIcke'sin, katotwut otI kcIsiwno kamIsh ike' kishpIn ke'itume'k otI e'pkotniak,KikshkansI, ipi wupukson shi kcukumik, ike'nomkuk.
40N||21||22||Ipi cak ke'ko we'kwe'ntuk ke'ntotmowe'kwe'n numaie'k, te'pwe'ie'ntume'k iwsu ke'shuminkoie'k.
40N||21||23||Pic cI kapitike't shi kcI-nume'okumkok, ki kcI me'matmocIk ipi ki oke'ctaosunmwan kinIshInape'k, kipie'naskakon, me'kwa e'ie'kinomake't, otI cI okinawan, TInipi we'tnumIn, otI wishkIswun otI e'shIcke'n? We'ni cI ke' kaminkon otI wishkIswun?.
40N||21||24||IcI Cisus okinkwe'twan otI cI okinan, Ninke' kInatonum nkot ke'ko; kishpIn cI witmoie'k, ninke' kuwitmonum we'tnuman otI wishkIswun we'ctotman.
40N||21||25||Iw kIctapie'nwe'wun o Can; tInipi cI we'piamkuk, shpumukinI tanake' nInik? IcI e'kinatatwat otI kikItwuk, KishpIn otI kItie'kon, shpumuk sI otI kukonan, TacIshIna kapwao cI te'pwe'twe'k.
40N||21||26||KishpIn cI kItie'kon; ni nInwun, kokwIsamIn ki nIshInape'k, osam caye'k ote'ne'nmawan ni CanIn ke'cwa nakanacimot.
40N||21||27||Okinkwe'twawan cI ni CisusIn, otI okinawan, co nkuke'ntusimIn; icI otI okinan; Cosu ke'nin ku‘witmosnonum, otI we'tnaman ot nwishkIswun we'k totman otI.
40N||21||28||TInicI e'ne'ntume'k? Nkot nInI kinish win, okwIsun icI e'kinaskawIt, ni ke'ctaosincIn, otI cI okinan, NkwIs, wumikice'win e'kom e'kishkiwuk, shi nsiwonokamshI ktukanuk.
40N||21||29||Okinkwe'twan cI, otI okikon, Coin; icI shkIc kikisate'ntum, icI e'kishiat.
40N||21||30||Okinaskawan cI ni e'kacinIncIn, icI nasapkinan, icI okinkwe'twan otI okikon, NkIshia sI Nos, cocI kishie'si.
40N||21||31||We'nicI, ki nish kashIcke't osIn kashIntuwe'n mukot? OtI cI okinawan; Ke'ctaosItsI. Cisus cI otI okinan, We'we'nI ktInum, kimaocIke'onInwuk, ipi kiwaonIshkaiuk, kupitike'k otokumauwunuk Kshe'mIne'to kinwa e'pwamshu pitike'ie'k.
40N||21||32||Can kipie' kuke'nakakwa i, we'we'nI shiwe'psowun, co cI nIsh kite'pwe'twasiwa; kicI wi maocIshke'onInwuk, ipi ki waonIshkaiuk kite'pwe'twawan, icI kinwa kakish waptume'k, co kikisate'ntusinI i e'wite'pwe'twe'k.
40N||21||33||PsItumok, minI nkot iacimowIn, Ke'iapI nkot we'towikwamIt kaktukatuk, siwnokamIsh ktukan, ipi okiwakaan, kiwtaiukwan, ipi okiwankatan watsho oshItot shomnapo, ipi kiwshIton wikwam e'shpianuk, okiwaancI ktukie'wunInwan, icI pe'noc e'ki shumacit, otanuk.
40N||21||34||Cikiaukwan cI pic e'wikishkInuk i micum, okinokanan opmitakiamIn e'ci iInIt ni ktukie' onInwun e'wi wtapnumwat i micum.
40N||21||35||KicI ktukie' onInwuk okimshunawan, niw opmitakaimIn, nkot cI ni okipsItie'wawan, icI nkot cI niw okinsawan, ipi nkot sInie'n okipkamawan.
40N||21||36||MinI pe'kansIncIn, okinokanan opmitakaimIn wusimI ni kitshin, icI ni ne'tum nasap cI, ke' niw kitotwawan.
40N||21||37||Shkwe'iak cI, okinokanan ni okwIsun, otI cI kikIto, Okupite'nmawan sI nkwIsun.
40N||21||38||Pic cI ki ktukie' onInwuk kawapmawat ni okwIsnInIn otI kinItwuk, OtI sie'o shakwune't; aw nsatan, kinan cI ke'tpe'ntamIn i te'pe'ntukipIn.
40N||21||39||IcI e'kimshInawat, ipi okisakcIwe'pInawan shi siwnokam shI ktukanuk, icI e'kinsawat.
40N||21||40||Pic cI pie't te'pe'ntuk i siwnokamshI ktukan; tInicI ke'napnInat notI ktukie' onInwun,
40N||21||41||OtI cI okinawan, okukokwansukIne'nan sI ni mcInInwun pe'kansIncIn ni ktukie' onInwun okuwuan i siwnokamshI ktukan, ke'monkocIn i micum e'tso kishkInuk.
40N||21||42||Cisus cI otI okinan, ConI wika otI kiwatusinawa mIsInukInuk, I sIn kiwe'shke'cuk kaianwe'ntumwat iw ie'i ke'ne'tmIsuk shi e'wikwe'iak. Kshe'mIne'to sIiw otIshcIke'wun kumamkasaptamIn cI.
40N||21||43||Iw sI otI we'cne'nkon otokumauwun, Kshe'mIne'to, kuotapnamakom icI kuminak ki nIshInape'k ke'pie'tocuk i micumowun.
40N||21||44||We'kwe'ntuk cI ke'pmukocnokwe'n shi sInik, kupikwshIn, ipi we'kwe'ntuk cI ke'tsoskwe'n, kupisposo.
40N||21||45||Pic cIki, kcI-me'matmocIk onInwuk, ipi Pe'nisiuk, kanotmoat ni iacmonIn, okikuke'ntanawa, winwa e'kowat.
40N||21||46||Pic cI wamshInawat okikwsawan, ni maoce'tincIn Nakanacimot Osam winwa okine'nmawan.
40N||22||1||CISUS cI okinkwe'twan, otI okinan, minI ni acimonIn otI kItwe'k;
40N||22||2||Okumauwun i shpumuk, otI e'ne'ntakwuk ke'cwa nkot okuma kaoshInwiat okwIsIn, e'wi wiwunIt;
40N||22||3||Okimace'nashkawan, ni opmitakaimIn, e'wintomanIt ni wakumIncIn; co cI kipie'sin.
40N||22||4||MinI cI pe'kansIncIn ni opmitakaimIn, okimace'nashkawan, otI cI okinan, Wuwitmowuk kiwakmIcIk, PInI, shiI nkishwshuston i naokwe' wisnuwun, mpIshkimuk, ipi wanoukuk kishInsawak; ipi cake'ko nkishwshuston, pie'shiak sI nwikwke'wunuk.
40N||22||5||Ke'koishukcI okine'ntanawa icI pape'kan e'kishishiawat; nkot otItshI ktukie'wunuk, kishiI ocI ke' nkot e'tshe'tawe't.
40N||22||6||KicI kashkwicuk OkimshInawan niw OpmitakaimInIn, ipi na‘okitotwawan, icI e'kinsawat.
40N||22||7||Pic cI o kcI okuma kanotake't, i ki kcInshkatsI, okinInashkawan cI ni otI shumaknIshimIn, e'kiwnusanIt ni kanshowe'ncIn, ipi okicaksumwawan, iw ototanInIn.
40N||22||8||IcI okinan, ni opmitakaimIn, shiI sI kishwsusIn, i wikwtowIn, kicI kawikmIcuk copite'ntakwsIsik,
40N||22||9||Shiak ntoac ipI mie'wuk; tsocI ke'mkowe'kwe'n, ku‘wikmawak.
40N||22||10||IcI ki pmitakaiuk e'kishiawat shi mie'wuk, icI e'ki maote'nawat, caye'k tso kamkawawat, niw me'iashowe'psIncIn, ipi me'noshowe'psIncIn; icI kite'pse'k shi e'tshi wikwtuk.
40N||22||11||Pic, cI okcI okuma kapitike't, e'pie'wapmat, ni kawikmacIn, okiwapman, nkot nInIwun shi e'iInIt kapwa piskumnIt wikwtatikwowun.
40N||22||12||OtI cI okinan, Nikan tacI kapie'shupitike'n, e'pwa piskumIn i wikwtatikwowun? CocI okIshkitosin e'wi kikitot.
40N||22||13||IwcI kanat, o kcI okuma ni opmitakaimIn, TkopInuk one'cik osItik, ipi maciwunuk, ipi wupukinuk, me'kwe' kiskupkonia, shi e'tnIte'mok ipi e'tnwe'iapte'shnuk.
40N||22||14||Mce'sh ntomak; nIshcI puke'ci we'napmak.
40N||22||15||IcI okiwutshItanawa ki Pe'nisiuk, washI nkwapnawat, shiw okikitonuk.
40N||22||16||OkinInashkawawan cI e'ciiIt ni ke'knomowacIn, ipi ni Knotiunun, otI e'wi nunanIt, Ke'knomakIn nkuke'ntamIn tpasI e'shuwe'psin ipi we'we'nI e'shknomake'n o Kshe'mIne'to otIshcIke'wun ipi co ke'wIiI kitupate'nmasi,
40N||22||17||WitmoshInak e'ne'ntumIn? Ntamno shIcke'mInI minkIt Sisu i maocIcke'wun tanake' co?
40N||22||18||Cisus cI okike'ntumwan iomIcshowe'psiwnInawa otI okinan, We'kwnicI we'ckwcItupe'nmie'k, e'nume'kasie'k?
40N||22||19||WaptIIshuk i tpaomatwun i shonia. Nkot shInIn cI kipie'twawan.
40N||22||20||OtI cI okinan; We'nicI otI e'shnakwsIt; ipi we'npie'kasot?
40N||22||21||OtI cI okikon, Sisu sI. IcI otI okinan, Minuk Sisu tso te'pe'ntuk Sisu; ipi minuk Kshe'mIne'to tso tpe'ntuk o Kshe'mIne'to.
40N||22||22||IcI kanotmowawat i kakItnIt, kimamkate'ntumwuk, ipi okinknawan, icI e'kimaciwat.
40N||22||23||MinI cI i e'kishkiwuk kipie'naskakon ni Se'cwsiIn, ki e'kitocIk, cowIiI taiapsisi icI e'kinatawat.
40N||22||24||OtI okinawan, Ke'knomake'n, Mosus kikito, KishpIn nInI npot, pwa onicansIt, wikane'iIn cI taowiwunIn ni wiwun; e'wiw cI onicansItmowat ni wi kane'ipIninIn. 
40N||22||25||Ki ipIninIn sI e'cIiIiak, nouk ki shik we'wikane'ite'cuk, ocI ke'ctaosIt kauwiwut kinpo, icI e'pwanicansIt, okinkItmowan ni wiwun wikane'iIn.
40N||22||26||IcI ke' winwa caye'k okiianke'owiwmawan caye'k nouk katshIcIk.
40N||22||27||IcI mamo shkwe'iak o kwe' kinpo winke'?
40N||22||28||Pic cI iapsishnowat, we'ninIncI ke'wiwmukocIn ni nouk, caye'k e'ki wiwmukot.
40N||22||29||Cisus cI okinkwe'twan, otI okinan, KiwaonIshnomsI, e'pwakuke'ntume'k, i msInukIn, ipi i wishkIswun Kshe'mIne'to.
40N||22||30||Pic sI iapsishnuk, cowiwsik, ipi co mintusik wiwtowun nasap sI e'ne'ntakwsInIt ni omIshInuwe'mIn o Kshe'mIne'to shi shpumuk, iw se' e'ne'ntakwse'wat.
40N||22||31||OtI cI wi iapsishkuk kanocuk, conI kiwaptusinawa i msInukInuk i kashu knonkoie'k o Kshe'mIne'to, otI e'kitot?
40N||22||32||Nin sI Nto Kshe'mIne'to iumuk E'pIne'e'm, ipi Nto Kshe'mIne'to iumuk AysIk, ipi Nto Kshe'mIne'to iumuk Ce'kap, Cosu wi Kshe'mIne'to oto Kshe'mIne'to omukwsin ni ne'poncIn, mtIno ie'k pe'matsIncIn.
40N||22||33||Pic cI kimaoce'ticuk kanotwawat Kimamkate'ntumwawan, iw okukie'kwe'wunInIn.
40N||22||34||Pic cI ki Pe'nIsiuk kanotmoat, niw e'kiwaonmanIt ni Se'cwsiIn, kimaoce'tik; e'ciInIt.
40N||22||35||Ice' nkot ni tpakwnuke'onInI, okinatakon i natatwun, e'wikwcIte'pe'nmukot, otI cI okikon?
40N||22||36||Ke'knomake'n, TIni cI ie'i kcI kie'kwe'wun shi tpakwnuke'wunuk.
40N||22||37||Cisus cI otI okinan, Tpash o Te'pe'nmukwiIn, Kshe'mIne'to, caye'k shi kte'ik, ipi caye'k shi kcipamuk, ipi caye'k shi ktIne'ntumwunuk.
40N||22||38||OtI se' ie'i kie'kwe'wun ne'tmIsuk, ipi ke'c pite'ntakwuk.
40N||22||39||IcI i e'nishuk ike'win e'ne'ntakwuk, Tpash kic pmatsi e'shtpantusiIn.
40N||22||40||IwsI notI nish kie'kwe'wunIn e'cIkote'k, caye'k tpakwnuke'wun, ipi i nakanacimonIn.
40N||22||41||Me'kwace' e'maoce'tiwat ki Pe'nisiuk Cisus okinatawan.
40N||22||42||OtI Okinan; TInicI e'ne'nme'k o Knayst? We'ninIncI we'kwIsmukwocIn? otI cI okinawan, Te'pItsI, otokwIsnun.
40N||22||43||OtI cI okinan, We'kwnicI Te'pIt kaoce'shInkanat shi KcI cipamuk Te'pe'nmIt, otI e'kikItot?
40N||22||44||O Kshe'mIne'to otI okinan, Te'pe'nmIt, cipitupIn shi nte'pniwnak, nash kiwshukwa ki me'iane'nmukwie'nuk namiukwan ksItik.
40N||22||45||KishpIn Te'pIt ishuwawinat Te'pe'nmin tInicI e'shaokwIsmat.
40N||22||46||CocI wIiI nInI okikshkItosin washIiaishe'mat, icI i e'kikishkiwuk wIiI nInI cominI ke'ko okishI natawasiwan.
40N||23||1||ICI e'kiknonat Cisus ni maocatincIn, ipi ni ke'knomoacIn;
40N||23||2||OtI kikito, kisI We'npie'ke'cuk, ipi ki Pe'nisiuk cipitupwuk shi Mosus o cipitupwunuk,
40N||23||3||Caye'k cI we'kwe'ntuk kie'shI kie'kumukuwe'kwe'n, iw ke'shI naktuwe'ntume'k ipi i ke'totme'k, ke'kowi i shIcke'ke'kon, i e'shcIke'wat kItwuk sI mtIno cocowi i shIcke'sik.
40N||23||4||NapItmake'k sI ni wiwsha‘wunIn kwe'skonuk e'wipmotmuk, icI shi e'towawat otInmaknInuk ninInwun, winwa cowi co e'winmatnumwat tIna nkot onIciwan.
40N||23||5||E'wiwipmukwat sI ni nInwun, i caye'k we'cnInkie'wat; ipi omukite'tonawan ke'ni wiasotkwe'psonawan ipi omukite'tonawan ni se'kacknIn shiw piskumwakInawak.
40N||23||6||Ipi, ome'nwe'ntanawa e'shpI oshIckate'nuk, e'tshI wikwtowut, ipi ni nakansIncIn e'ci cipitupnIt, shi nume'okumkok.
40N||23||7||Ipi e'numkotwa shiw e'tshutatuk, ipi e'wikowat ni nInwun, Ke'knomake't, Ke'knomake't.
40N||23||8||Ke'ko wi kinwa, Ke'knomake', ShInkaske'k, mtIno nkot we' Ke'knomakwie'k Knayst cI o kinwacI caye'k ktowikane'itum.
40N||23||9||Ke'ko wi wIiI nInI Nos shInkanake'k shotI kik nkotwe' mtIno Koswa shpumuk e'iIt, kishkok.
40N||23||10||Ke'kowike' Te'pe'nke't, shInkaske'kon, nkot wI Te'pe'nmukwie'k o Knayst,
40N||23||11||We'kwe'ntuk ke'cI pite'ntakwsIt kinwa, oie'o ke'pmitakaiwut.
40N||23||12||We'kwe'ntuk ke' ke'kcI pite'ntuk wia‘w, oie'o ke'niswe'ntakwsIt, ipi ke'o ke'psuwe'ntuk wia‘w oie'o ke'kcI pite'ntakwsIt.
40N||23||13||Kokwansukumuk kinwa we'npie'ke'ie'k, ipi kinwa Pe'nisiuk, e'nume'kasie'k! kikupakwumwawa kinInwuk shpumuk iw okumauwun, cocke' kinwa tpInwe' kpitike'sim, coke' kitine'nmasiwak wanmupitike'cuk e'wi pitike'wat.
40N||23||14||Kokwansukumuk kinwa we'npie'ke'ie'k, ipi kinwa Pe'nisiuk e'nume'kasie'k; kcakitumwawak shakaocIk, otowikwamwam, ipi nIsh knoe'sh ktItnankitonum, e'mumatumoie'k; iwcI i kotIskonawa wusimI mIcitotatwun.
40N||23||15||Ko kwansukumuk sI kinwa we'npie'ke'ie'k, ipi kinwa Pe'nisiuk, e'nume'kasiuk! kiwtashkanawa i kcukum, ipi ikI, e'wimkowe'k nkot, wawitokwe'k, pic cI witokone'k, nishuk wusimI kitIshawa win, onicansumkot shi namkumuk, icI kinwa e'shwe'psie'k.
40N||23||16||Kokwansukumuk kinwa ke'kie'pikwaie'k nakanwusie'k, otI e'kItie'k, We'kwe'ntuk ke'kie'tnamtakwsukwe'n, i kcI nume'okumuk, coke'ko nomkIsnon, we'kwe'ntuk cie'k ke'kie'tnamtakwsukwe'n i osawshonia kcInumie'okumkok, kawite'pwe'.
40N||23||17||Kukie'patsIm, ipi kukie'pikwam, We'kwni cI wusimI e'pite'ntakwuk i osawshonia tanake' i kcInume'okumuk we'c te'pe'ntakwuk i osawshonia?
40N||23||18||Ipi we'kwe'ntuk ke'kie'tnamtakwsukwe'n shi e'tshipitakwe'k, coke'ko nomkIsnon we'kwe'ntukie'k ke' kie'tnamtakwsukwe'n i kie'pitakwe'k, ka‘wite'pwe'.
40N||23||19||Kukie'patsIm, ipi kukie'pikwam, We'kwni cI wusimI e'pite'ntakwuk, ipatakwe'k, tanake' i e'tshI pitakwe'k, te'pe'ntuk i pitakwe'wun.
40N||23||20||Wikwe'ntuke' ke'kie'tnamtakwsukwe'n, shi e'tshi pitakwe'k, ke'kie'tnamtakwsu shi ipi ni caye'k ke'ko kwIciukwan e'te'nuk.
40N||23||21||Ipi we'kwe'ntuk ke'kie'tnamtakwsukwe'n i kcI nume'okumuk ke'kie'tnamtakwsu, ipi ni shi pituk e'inIncIn.
40N||23||22||Ipi we'kwe'ntuk ke'kie'tnamtakwsukwe'n, shi shpumuk kishkok, ke'kie'tnamtakwsu shi Kshe'mIne'to Ocipitupwun, ipi ni shi capitupnIt.
40N||23||23||Kokwansukumuk kinwa we'npie'ke'ie'k, ipi kinwa, Pe'nisiuk, e'nume'kasie'k! me'tatsukIn kitpumakIn, i mInIt ipi e'nIs, ipi kumIn, icI kiswe'tonawa ke'c pite'ntakwukIn, i tpakwnuke'e'wun; shuwe'ntuwun, ipi te'pwe'ne'ntumwun; notI sI i e'ni takitotme'k; cocI ktakinkItsinawan i nomkukipIn.
40N||23||24||Ke' kie'pikwaie'k nakaniie'k! e'cikwakmIshkane'k, nIshpukos, icI wi e'kme'k kco we'si.
40N||23||25||Kokwansukumuk kinwa, we'npie'ke'ie'k, ipi, kinwa Pe'nisiuk e'nume'kasie'k, kinwa kpintonawa Sakiciiukwan i mnukwackIn, ipi i onakIn, shi cowi pic iukwan moshkine'mkIt wie'shke'wun, ipi me'anuk.
40N||23||26||Kin ke'kie'pikwan e' Pe'nisiwin! Pinakwton ne'tum, shi piciukwan i mnukwackIn, ipi onakIn, icI shi sakici iukwan ke' kupinakwton.
40N||23||27||Kokwansukumuk kinwa, we'npie'ke'ie'k ipi kinwa Pe'nisiuk, e'nume'kasie'k! ke'cwa kinwa e'shnakwse'ie'k i wapshkIckate'k cipe'‘okumkwe'n, we'we'nI e'mnwapme'nakwuk sakici iukwan shi ca‘wi pic iukwan moshkIne'ton ne'pcuknInwuk otoknimwan, ipi caye'k wanakwuk.
40N||23||28||IusukI kinwa; nasap sakici iukwan kte'napme'nakwsum me'noshuwe'psukIn e'wi napmukwie'k nInwuk, piciukwan ca‘wi kmoshknIstonawa nume'kaswun, ipi mIcIshuwe'psuwun.
40N||23||29||Kokwansukumuk kinwa, we'npie'ke'ie'k, ipi kinwa, Pe'nisiuk e'nume'kasie'k! kitoshtawawak maokiocipe'‘kumukom-wan, ki nakanacimocuk ipi kiakume'tum-wawak, ni ocipe'‘kumukomwan ki ne'pwaka pIninuk.
40N||23||30||OtI e'kItie'k kishpIn ie'iakpIn e'ie'pmatsuwat nosnanuk, contakinatmoasimIn, pic ne'sawat ni nakanacimoncIn.
40N||23||31||TInicI kwawintusom sI kinwa, e'winicansumkoie'k kikansacuk nakanacimoncIn.
40N||23||32||MoshkInitok sI i, otpukInwan kikoswak.
40N||23||33||MIntoie'k; iaianke' pmatsie'k pwatacke'ie'kme'ntoie'k tInicI ke'cI ktIski-ie'k shi pnatsowun namkumuk: shkote'k?
40N||23||34||PInI, kipukite'nmonum ki nakanacimocuk ipi ne'pwakacuk nInwuk, ipi we'npie'ke'cuk, anIt cI kInsawak, ipi kIskakwawak, anIt ke' kupsItie'wawak shi kte'nume'okumkowak, ipi kukwtukawak onukmuk otanuk.
40N||23||35||Kinwa cI ktakshkakwnawa piamkuk caye'k i maywakawun mskwI kasikwe'pnukate'k shotI kik, omuskwim E'pun, kanpwakat, nash mIskwim o Se'kinaye's kaokwIsmukot Pe'nukaye's, katpIne'k na‘oiukwan shi kcI-nume'okumkok, ipi shi e'tshi pitakwe'k.
40N||23||36||We'we'nI ktInum caye'k notI okupie'naskakwnawa kotI pe'matse'cuk.
40N||23||37||O Cinose'nam! Cinose'nam! kin kansItwa ki nakanacimocuk ipi e'ki pmIsInwutwa, ki kapkItnumakon; tunitsuk taki maotInkwa knicansuk, ke'cwa pkuakwa e'maotoshmat opunsha ne'imIn, namiukwan onukwiknuk; co cI kine'ntusinawa?
40N||23||38||PInI! ku wikwamwa kinukitumakom pe'pshukwu‘te'.
40N||23||39||OtI ktInum, Co wi minI kuwapmIsim, nash, pama otI kItie'k, MnawankosI o pie'iat shiw otunoswunuk Kshe'mIne'ton.
40N||24||1||CISUS cI kisakum kiw cImaci shi kcInume'okumkok; nicI e'knomowacIn, okipie'naskakon e'wiwaptukot e'shcI kate'nuk i kcI nume'okumuk.
40N||24||2||Cisus cI otI okinan, kuwaptanawa nI caye'k notI? We'we'nI kItInum, Co wi nkot sIn kwucie'kwan kte'snon, caye'k kniswe'pnukate'ton.
40N||24||3||Ka cipitupIt shi e'pkotnianuk Anipik, e'knomowacIn cI kimoc okipie'naskakon, otI cI okikon, WitmoshInak tapicI otI ike'nomkuk? ipi E'ni cI ke'shu kInwa sapmnakwuk pic wipian? ipi i washu kInwasapmnakwuk pic wishkwakiwuk?
40N||24||4||Cisus cI okinkwe'twan, otI okinan akwamsuk sI owIiI nInI e'wipwawie'shmukwie'k.
40N||24||5||Cumane'k sI ntunoswunuk ke'pie' shiacuk otI kukItwuk, Nin su Knayst; icI mce'sh ke'cowie'shmat.
40N||24||6||Ipi Knotanawa i mikatwunun, ipi ianmukumukuk, i mikatwunIn, ikwamsuk kcI e'wipwa mkoshkate'ntume'k iwsI caye'k notI ke'showe'puk, icI wi e'wishkwuakiwuk; comshI pie'mkIsnon.
40N||24||7||Kupsukwik cI papukan e'shumcuk ke'cI mikatwat, ipi papukan okumawunIn, ipi kukicupikIte'kiwun ipi kukicI iakwnoke'kiwun, ipi knanImshke' onukmuk nkoci kI.
40N||24||8||IwsI caye'k notI we'cmacimkuk mkoshkate'ntumwunIn.
40N||24||9||IwcI pic ke'cipkItnukoie'k, shi watshI kwtukukoie'k, ipi kInsukom, ipi kshike'nmukwak caye'k e'tsoshumocuk nin ke'o te'nmukoie'k ntInoswunuk.
40N||24||10||IwcI pic mce'sh kInshke'ntik, ipi kawie'shtik, ipi onukumuk kIshI shi ke'ntik.
40N||24||11||Ipi kumane'k ke'psukwicuk nakanacimokascuk mce'sh cI okawie'shmawan.
40N||24||12||McI showe'psowun cI osam e'mane'k mce'sh cI tpantowun kItkIsnunI.
40N||24||13||WincI pIne' ke'iakwamsIt oie'o ke'ke'skonIt,
40N||24||14||Ipi otI okumauwun mnoacmowIn ke'iacIkate' caye'k shotI kik, ke'kI kukInwa te'ntumwat caye'k e'tso shumocuk, icI ke'cI piamkuk e'wishkwakiwuk.
40N||24||15||Pic cI wapmie'k ki shake'ntakwse'cuk ke'pnactocuk, kashInikanacimot nakanacimot Te'niunIn, ni pwowat shi e'tshe'mno shIcke'wat (we'kwe'ntuk ke'waptumkwe'n shiw msInukInuk uocma okInsItan,)
40N||24||16||IcI ki ke'ie'cuk Cwtie'uk, nocma knInshumwuk, shi e'cI pkotnianuk.
40N||24||17||Winke' o kwItIpuk e'iIt co kupie'nisasisi e'wiwtapnuk ke'ko shi wikwamuk.
40N||24||18||Winke' o ktIkanuk ke'iIt cocupie'kiwe'si e'wiwtapnuk otikwame'iIn.
40N||24||19||Kukokwansuksik ki ke'ncukwcuk, ipi ki ke'nonaosocuk, shi niw e'kishkiwuk.
40N||24||20||Numak e'wi pwapomkuk pic oshumie'k nainIta ke' e'wipwa nume'kishkuk.
40N||24||21||IwcI pic ke'cu kcI ianmukiwuk, cowikakinomkIsnon e'kowe'pkiwuk, otI pic coke' minI i knomkIsnon.
40N||24||22||KishpIn sI notI e'kishkiwuk pke'ci shIckate'k, co wIiI pe'matsIt kuke'skonasi; kiw cie'k we'we'napcukascuk, e'kishkiwuk ke'ocI, pke'ciw shItok.
40N||24||23||KishpIn sI wIiI nInI otIkoie'k, PInI otukw‘shI Knayst, Tanake' ako, ke'ko tpwe'twake'k.
40N||24||24||Kupsukwik kwshI nIsh Knayst ke'shInkatsocIk, ipi nakanacimokascuk, ipi kuwaptuukowak kawimataonokie'k e'wimamkate'ntakwsIwat, kishpIn cI kshkItowat nike' otawie'shmawan ni kaowe'napcIkasnIncIn.
40N||24||25||PInI kisha sI kowitmonum.
40N||24||26||KipIn cI wIiI otukoie'k, PInI, ipI sI iuwak na, wiukwan, ke'ko ipI shiake'k, PInI kimoc iawak shi wikwamuk ke'ko wi te'pwe'twake'k.
40N||24||27||Ke'cwa pwawasmok e'wcipiamkuk we'cmokuk, ipi e'wawase'shkuk nash ipI we'cpkIshmok, iw sI ke'nomkuk pic piat We'kwIsmukot NInwun.
40N||24||28||E'ciiukwe'n ne'pot, wiio’w, shiw ce'ci maoce'tiwat ki knowuk.
40N||24||29||Kie'nup cI kikishianmukiwuk, ni kishkiwunIn, kisIs ke'o kukisupkoniawapmnakwsI; ipi tpuk kisIs co kawawase'shkmake'si, ipi ki nukok shpumuk kaotukocnok, ipi nishke'e'osawunIn ipI shpumuk kInukshke'non.
40N||24||30||IcI pic ke'cinakwte'nuk otI kinwaciawun o We'kwIsmukot NInwun shiw shpumuk, iwcI ke'ki caye'k e'tsoshumowat, shotI kik kukitImake'nmok, ipi kowapmawan, ni We'kwIsmImcIn NInwun pie'tnIsnIt ankwotok, shi shpumuk, okupie'iIn cI okIshkIe'wsowun, ipi okcImnowankoswun.
40N||24||31||IcI ke'cI pie'mace'nashkawat omIshInIwe'mIn kupie' kcI notakwtonawa i notakwcIkIn, icI ke'cI maotonawat, win kawe'napmacIn e'nkokwak otI kI.
40N||24||32||Mpe' wi kuke'ntumok iaiacimowIn i cIsiwnokamIsh, pic saknumkwicIn shiw otukwasuk, ipi sakpuksicIn kukuke'ntanawa shiI ci kiukwan e'mnokumuk.
40N||24||33||IwsI kinwa pic waptme'k caye'k notI kukne'tmok e'cikiukwanwuk shishkwate'muk.
40N||24||34||We'we'nI KtInum; Cowi kumacisik kotI pe'matse'cuk, pama caye'k notI kitpIsak.
40N||24||35||Kishuk ipi cI, kupinaca, otIie'k ntuktowun co kupnacasnon.
40N||24||36||Pic i e'kishkiwuk, ipi tupukIn, co wIiI okuke'ntusin, nInI mocki co mIshInwe'k ipI shpumuk mtIno ie'k Nos.
40N||24||37||Ka nomkItInuk Noe', okishkomIn, i sI ke'win nasap, ke'nomkItInuk piat o We'kwIsmukot NInwun.
40N||24||38||Iw e'shkishkiwuk e'pwamshumoshkuk kiwisnik, ipi kimnukwe'k, kiwiwtik ipi kimamintik e'wi wiwtowat, nash i e'kishkuk, Noe' e'kiposIt shi napkwanuk.
40N||24||39||Co cI okike'ntusinawa nash e'moshkInuk kapiamkItInuk icI caye'k e'ki we'pokwat, iwsI nasap ke'nomkItInuk pic piat o We'kwIsmukot NInwun.
40N||24||40||Iw cI pic nish ke'ik ktukanuk nkot cI kaotapna, ocI nkot kInkIna.
40N||24||41||Nish kwe'k kupispotaswuk, shi potakunuk, nkot cI kaotapna, ocI nkot kInkIna.
40N||24||42||Kawapuk cI co ku ke'ntusinawa i tpukIn, pic ke'piat o Te'pe'nmukwie'k.
40N||24||43||Kuke'ntumok cI otI, KishpIn nInI te'pe'ntuk wikwam kuke'ntuk pic ke'mockIncIn wipianIt, otakawapman coke' otakine'ntusin ie'tat e'wipikw ukate'nuk.
40N||24||44||TInicI oshInwiksuke' kinwa, e'pwamshI shIte'aie'k kupie'wak We'kwIsmukot NInwun.
40N||24||45||We'ni cI iakwamsIt, ipi ne'pwakat pmitaka kaokmaoukot ni te'pe'nmukocIn shi e'tat e'wiminat wisnuwun mno opi?
40N||24||46||KIshuwe'ntakwsI su o pmitaka, pic pianIt ni te'pe'nmukwocIn mkumakot i shIcke't.
40N||24||47||We'we'nI sI otI KtInum, okItIpIntumokon caye'k i otupunowe'wsowun.
40N||24||48||KishpIn ke' o me'iashuwe'psIt pmitaka, ote'‘ik cI otI kitot, Te'pe'nmIt kcukinowe'sh e'pwamshupiat.
40N||24||49||IcI ke'cI we'pwe'potwat wic pmitakaiIn, ipi witopmat, ipi mnukwe't, ni kawshkwe'pie'ncIn.
40N||24||50||Te'pe'nmukwocIn o pmitaka kupie'n e'kishkiwnunuk, e'pwam shI ntawapme't pic ke' i tpukInuk e'pwamshI pame'nmat.
40N||24||51||Okukishkokon cI, ipi okupukinukon e'ciInIt ni e'nume'kasnIncIn, shi cI ke'tne'te'mok ipi ke'tnwe'iapte'shnuk.
40N||25||1||OTI sI ke'ne'ntakwuk shpumuk okumawIn Ke'cwa mtatso, she'shksiuk, kaotapnumwat ni Wase'ncIkInumwan, icI e'ki wunkwe'shkwawat we'shkuwi winIncIn.
40N||25||2||NianIn cI ki, kinpwakak, kicI nianIn kikie'patsik.
40N||25||3||KicI kakie'patse'cuk pe''pshuk okimacitonawan wase'ncIknumwan, cocI i pmIte' okimacitosinawa.
40N||25||4||Ne'pwakacuk ie'k okimacitonawa pmIte', pic iukwan otutaswunwak, ipi ni wase'ncIknumwan.
40N||25||5||E'pwamshIpianIt ni we'shkwi wunIncIn, caye'k ki note' npe'k,
40N||25||6||IcI e'iaptItpukuk okinotanawa otI e'kcI notakwtunuk, PInI, owe'shkwiwut shiI pie'wak; Shiak we'nkwe'shkowuk.
40N||25||7||IcI kotI caye'k she'shksiuk, e'kipsukwiwat e'kina' towat wase'ncIkunumwan.
40N||25||8||IcI ki ke'kie'patse'cuk, okinawan ni ne'pwakancIn mishInak i kpumte'mwa, osam ninan nwase'ncIk e'numnanIn iate'on.
40N||25||9||KicI napwakacuk okin kwe'twawan, otI okinawan; Coin, cotanak tate'pse'snon kinwa, e'wi ie'ie'k, ipi ninan, kitashiam e'tshu tatuk, ipi kita kishpIne'tatsom.
40N||25||10||IcI pic e'ie'shiawat e'wu kishpIne'towat, kipie'n owe'shkwiwinIncIn, ipi kapwiacuk okinmowice'wawan e'kipitke'nsht shi watshI owiwunIt icI i shkwate'm e'kikpakwukate'k.
40N||25||11||Pama; ke'winwa nakIc kipie'k kianIt she'shksiuk; otI cI kikItwuk Te'pe'nmiak, Te'pe'nmiak, nsakwunumwushnak.
40N||25||12||Okinkwe'twan cI, otI okinan; We'we'nI ktInum; Cokuke'nmIsnonum.
40N||25||13||KuwapuksI co kuke'ntusinawa, i e'kishkiwuk, tankake', tpukIn, pic ke'piat We'kwIsmukot NInwun.
40N||25||14||OtIsI e'ne'ntakwuk iw okumauwun shpumuk kishkok; ke'cwa nInI, e'wipamatsIt, pnoc e'shiatotanuk; e'kintomat opmitakaimIn, icI e'kiswe'nmowat, otInkackIn.
40N||25||15||Nkot cI okimiman, Nianuk mtatswak tso shonia; icI minI nkot, nishuk mtatswak tso shonia, icI minI nkot, nkotuk mtatswak tso shonia; e'ne'ntakwse'nIt sI okinu'onan icI papuk ki maci.
40N||25||16||IcI ke'win kaminIt, Nianuk mtatswak tso shonia, kiwutawe'i, icI e'kiwtutuuk minI wusimI nianuk mtatswak tso shonia.
40N||25||17||Winke' nishIk mtatswak kaminIt, winke' nishIk mtatswak, wusimI okiiIn.
40N||25||18||IcI ke'wi o kaminIt nkotuk mtatswak kishie'wak icI e'kiwanke't ukik, e'kikItwat te'pe'nmukocIn oshoniaimInIn.
40N||25||19||Pama cowika te'pe'nmat, notI pmitakaimIn kipie'; e'wike'nmat kanInkie'nIt,
40N||25||20||IcI o kaminIt nianuk mtatswak tso shonia, kipie'wak, okipie'ton nianuk mtatswak tso shonia wusimI; otIcI kikito, Te'pe'nmin, kimishInapIn nianuk mtatswak tso shonia, pInI wusimI nianuk mtatswak tso shonia, nkikshkIton.
40N||25||21||IcI ni te'pe'nmukocIn 'otI okikon, We'we'nI kitotum me'noshuwe'psin, ipi me'nototmIn pmitakIn, kimnototanIn; otI pke''cicoiIn mane'kIn kako kuminIn wakawakawaptumIn; Pitike'n e'tshI mnowankosIt te'pe'nmukwiIn.
40N||25||22||Winke' o kaminIt nishuk mtatswak tso shonia, kipie', otIcI, okinan; Te'pe'nmin, kimish nishuk mtatswak tso shonia; pInI wusimI nishuk mtatswak tso shonia, nkikshkIton.
40N||25||23||IcI ni te'pe'nmukocIn otI okikon We'we'nI kitotum me'noshuwe'psin, ipi me'nototmIn pmitakIn, kimnototanIn OtI pke''cikaiIn, mane'kIn ke'ko kuminIn wakawaptumIn; Pitike'n e'tshe' mnowankosIt, te'pe'nmukwiIn.
40N||25||24||IcI ke'wi o e'kipiat kaminIt nkotuk mtatswak tso shonia, otI cI okinan, Te'pe'nmin kike'nmIn, e'shsnuksiwnunwin, e'kishkIshke'n kacupwa swe'we'pnuke'n ipi e'maotInkIn kacupwa nisknukIn.
40N||25||25||Nkikwtac icI e'ki shiaie'n, ipi e'ki wukIto ian ikshoniaium, ne'kwukik, pInI otI cI kte'iIn te' pe'ntumIn.
40N||25||26||Te'pe'nmukocIn okinkwe'takon, otI cI, oki kon, E'ukie'patIs, ipi kiapie'tus, pmitaka, kike' num, e'kish kshkuke'ian kacupwa swe'we'pnuke'ian, ipi e'naotInke'ian kacupwa swe'we'pnuke'ian, ipi e'maotInke'ian kaucupwapmnisknIke'ian.
40N||25||27||Kitakiwuton sIi nshoniam ki iashtonke'cIk, piaiancI ntaki tkotapinan te'pe'ntuman ipi i takikshkIcke'mkukIpIn.
40N||25||28||OtapInImak i nkotuk mtatswak tso shonia, icI minuk i e'iIt mtatsuk mtatswak tso shonia.
40N||25||29||We'kwe'ntuksI e'ie'kwe'n kumina, icI mce'sh ke'ciIt, ocI ke'pwaiIt, kaotapnumwa ike'ian nwe'iIt.
40N||25||30||Pukinuk cI o ke'ko pwanaptIsIt pmitaka me'kwe' kiskupkonia e'tshI tnIte'mok, ipi e'tnwe'iapitshe'nuk.
40N||25||31||Pic cI We'kwIsmukot NInwun, kupie'wak okIcpite'ntakwsowunuk, ipi ni caye'k me'noshuwe'psIncIn omIshIne'we'mIn okupie'wice'okon, icI ke' cI cipitupIt okIcne'ntakwse'wunuk cipitupwunuk.
40N||25||32||IcI e'nasmupIt kumaotInkaswun cak e'shumInIt nIshInape'n; icI ke'cI papke'pnat; ke'cwa e'shpapke'pnat nInI omantanshImIn ipi nimotoiun.
40N||25||33||IcI ke'cI cipitupat nimantanshIn ote'pniwnak, nicI motoiIn onumciwnak.
40N||25||34||OtI cI okInan, KcI okuma niw e'inIt ote'pniwnak, Pie'macik she'winmukwie'k Nos, pitike'k okumauwunuk kaoshItakoie'k e'kowe'pkiwuk.
40N||25||35||Npukite'napInsI, icI e'kishumie'k; nkikakas kIte''e's, icI e'ki mnIie'k conkikuke'ncukasi, icI e'kipitkIshie'k.
40N||25||36||Nki shashakiti icI e'kikwe''ie'k, ipi nki iakwnoka, icI e'kipie'wapme'ie'k, nkikupakwukaske', icI e'ki pie'naskawie'k.
40N||25||37||IcI ke'cInkwe't-wawat ki me'noshuwe'pse'cIk, otI cI kukItwuk, Te'pe'nmiak, TapicI, kawapmInkon e'pkIte'n, icI e'shumnukon tanake' e'kakaskIte'-e'siIn, icI e'kimne''nukon.
40N||25||38||TapicI kawapme'nkon e'pwake'ncukasiIn, icI e'pitike'nkon tanake' e'shashakitin, icI e'kwe'inukoncI.
40N||25||39||TapicI kawapme'nkon e'iakwnokan, tanake', e'kupakokon, icI e'kipie' shi iIiak.
40N||25||40||IwcI KcI-okuma okinkwe'twan, otI cI okInan, We'we'nI, KtInum, otI e'kitotwe'k nkot otI mamwI kaciIt kotI ni kane'iuk, isI nasap e'totwe'ie'k Nin.
40N||25||41||OtI cI kie' win ni pic kie'nat e'inIncIn onumciwnak; Wus macik; e'pukicukasie'k kakuke' shkote'k, kaoshItwut mIcImIne'to, ipi niw omushIne'we'mIn.
40N||25||42||NkipkIte' cocI kishumsim; nkikakaskite'e's, cocI kimnIsim.
40N||25||43||Conkikike'ntakwsIsi, cocI kipitike'shsim, nkishashakiti, cocI kikwe''sim; nkiiakwnoka, ipi nkikpakwukas; cocI kimpoace'sim.
40N||25||44||IcI ke' ke'winwa ke'cInkwe'twawat otI okInawan, te'pe'nmiak, tapicI kawapmInkon e'pkIte'n tanake', e'kakaskIte'-e'siIn, tanake' e'pwake'ntakwsin tanake', e'shashakitin, tanake' e'iakwnkan tanake', e'kupakwukasiIn; cocI nkipmitosnonmIn.
40N||25||45||IcI ke' cInkwe'twat, otI cI okInan; We'we'nI KtInum, KashI pwatotwe'k nkot otI mamwI kaciIt; coi kitotwusim.
40N||25||46||KotIcI kishie'k kake' kwtuksonk; KotI cI ie'k me'noshuwe'pse'cuk kIshie'k kake' pmatsowunuk.
40N||26||1||ICI Cisus kakishkitot caye'k note', kikitonIn, otI okinan e'knomowacIn.
40N||26||2||Kuke'ntanawa kikish nish konkuk, ke'cI iashwe'sak wikwta‘wun iwcI We'kwIsmukot NInwun kupkIte'ncikaso e'wiskakwukasot.
40N||26||3||IcI e'kimaoce'‘tiwat, kcI-me'matmocuk onInimwan ipi ki we'npie'mowacuk, ipi oke'ctaosimwan, ki nIshInape'k, shi e'citanIt ni kcIme'matmot nInI e'shnukasot Ke'ie'pus.
40N||26||4||IcI e'kinatatwat, e'wiwie'shawat ni CisusIn, ipi e'winsawat.
40N||26||5||OtI cI kikItwuk, Coin nkom e'kishkiwuk e'wikwtuk, tanshonatkumkIswuk ki nIshIape'k.
40N||26||6||Me'kwa Cisus e'ie'iIt Pe'te'niuk shi e'tanIt Sayiman we'mkit.
40N||26||7||Kipie'naskakon e'ciIt kwe'n okipie'iIn, SInmkukos ke'cwunItnuk nmukwiwun, icI e'kisiknamakot otupik; me'kwa e'cipitupnIt e'ie'wisnInIt.
40N||26||8||IcI ni ke'knomowacIn kawaptumwawat, kinshkatsiwe'n tumwuk otI cI kikItwuk; TInicI e'napciak otI e'nshonac cIkate'k.
40N||26||9||OtI nmukwiwun tawe'‘kpIn mce'sh, takipite'ntakwut, icI takicI mintwa ke'tmakse'cuk,
40N||26||10||Pic cI Cisus kakwiuk kwe'nmat, otI okinan, We'kwnicI we'cmkoshkate'nme'k otI kwe'? Nme'nototak sI i e'totwut.
40N||26||11||PIne' kinwa kie'tmakse'cuk kpumiuwawak, nin ca‘ wi co pIne'‘ nte'‘isi.
40N||26||12||IwsI i e'kisiknuk otI nmukwiwun shi niiwukwe'ctotuk i e'winkokasian.
40N||26||13||We'we'nI KtInum; ke'pashiamkuk, i otI mInwacimowun, ke'iacukate', caye'k shotI kik; otIke', ke'iapI kwe' ke'iacIkate'ne' katotuk; e'wipwawaone'nciasot.
40N||26||14||IcI nkot kimtatso shItInish kashInkasot Cwte's Iske'niut, kishie'wak e'ciiInIt ni kcI me'matmocuk onInwun.
40N||26||15||OtI cI okinan, We'kwnicI tamishie'k ktapkItnumonum. IcI e'ki wawitmowawat nswapituk tso shonia.
40N||26||16||IcI iwpi e'ki kwinwune'ntuk washIpataat.
40N||26||17||IcI i e'ne'tmukishkuk iw wikwtowun opwaopuce'te'k pkwe'shkIn, ni ke'knomawacIn kipie'naskawawan CisusIn, otI cI okinawan TInipi cI ke'cI wa‘wshustoiak; i e'wimiciIn iashwe'saki wikwtowun.
40N||26||18||OtI cI okinan, Shiak kcI otanuk, nInI otI cI; knawa; Ke'knomake't kIto, Pe'shoc pie'mkIt, e'wimacian iashwe'sak wikwtowun shiw nke'‘iIn, i shi e'tan, ipi ki ke'knomokwa.
40N||26||19||IcI ni ke'knomowacIn kitotmok kakowat ni CisusIn; icI e'ki oshInwitowat, i iashwe'sak wikwtowun.
40N||26||20||IcI wanmupkonianuk okiwitpaman ni mtatso shItnish.
40N||26||21||IcI e'iI wisnawat otI kikito; We'we'nI KtInum, Nkote'iI kinwa kupataum.
40N||26||22||IcI kikcI kisate'ntumwuk icI e'we'p cacipnowe'‘ otI e'nawat, Te'pe'nke'n nin nI‘?
40N||26||23||E'kinkwe'twancI otI cI okinan, WinsI wacpmukamIt niw onIce'n shiw onakunuk, owiie'o ke'patamIt.
40N||26||24||We'kwIsmukot NInwun maciwok e'shpie'kasot; kokwan sukukumuk o nInI, pataat, ni We'kwIsmukot NInwun; wusimI takiwunIt o nInI wika pwanikpIt.
40N||26||25||IcI Cwte's kapataat okinkwe'twan otI cI okinan, Ke'knomakIn nin nI? IcI otI okinan KikishkItsI.
40N||26||26||IcI me'kwa e'iI wisne'wat Cisus okiw tapnan pkwe'shkIn, ipi kinume'; icI e'kipikupitot; icI e'kiminat, ni ke'knomowacIn, otI cI kikito, Otapne'mok micuk, otI ie'i niia‘w.
40N||26||27||Ipi okiwtapnan i mnukwackIn, ipi kiwawiiwe' icI e'kiminat otI okinan; Mnukwe'k i e'tshie'k.
40N||26||28||OtI ie'i nmIskwim oshkawawitmake'wnuk we'csikwe'pnukate'k mce'sh e'wi we'pnukate'nuk ome'iashuwe'psiwnawan.
40N||26||29||OtI cI ktInum, Cowi minI nkumnukwe'sin, e'micmowuk iw siwnokamIsh, pama i e'kishkiwuk, ke'cI oshku wic mnukwe'nmukon shi Nos otokumauwunuk.
40N||26||30||IcI kakish nkumwat i nkumwun; kisakumwuk, kishie'k shi e'pkotniak AnipIk.
40N||26||31||IcI Cisus otI okinan, Caye'k kinwa kInshke'nmIm nin, nkom e'pkoniak, otI e'shpie'kate'k; Nkuwe'potwa mantanshIn e'kwapmat, icI ki mantanshuk pe'msokapwucuk onukmuk ke'shI sowe'ptowat.
40N||26||32||IcI ki kish onIshkaian nkInmI‘ nikani, ipI Ke'ne'niuk.
40N||26||33||Pitu cI okinkwe'twan, OtI okinan, KishpIn msote' kaye'k nInwuk, nshke'nmukwiIn, coin nin nash ktanshke'nmIsnon.
40N||26||34||Cisus cI otI okinan; We'we'nI KtInum, nkom e'pkoniak e'pwamshI notakwsIt pkaukwa nsuk conkuke'nmasi kIshI.
40N||26||35||Pitu cI otI, okinan wic npotonan konkuke'nmasi coi ntakItsi, Nasap ke'ni caye'k okikon, nike'knomowacIn.
40N||26||36||IcI e'ki pie'wice'wat Cisus, e'kipie'shiawat shi Ke't-se'mIni e'shnukate'k otI cI okinan, ni ke'knomowacIn; Cipitupuk shotI e'ie' shiaian e'shi e'winumaian.
40N||26||37||OtInI macinan cI PituiIn ipi ni nish okwIsun Se'pe'ti, icI e'we'pme' nshonate'ntuk, ipi ki kcI kwsukwe'ntum.
40N||26||38||IcI otI okinan, Nin cipam kcI nshonate'ntum, ke'cwa npowIn; shotIiuk, ipi wic kawapmie'k.
40N||26||39||Pe'shoc cI wusimI kishiI; ipi kicicikwe'se', ipi kinume', otI cI kikito, O! Nose' kishpIn sI e'ne'ntumwune'n, nocma nkukwe'pmosankon otI mnukwackIn; Coin Nin e'ne'ntuman’ kin sI e'ne'ntumIn.
40N||26||40||Kipie' shie' cI ni ke'knomowcIn, okimakawan e'npanIt, otI cI okinan, ni PituiIn, TIni conukwnI ktanu kawapsim nkot tupkIn.
40N||26||41||Kuwapuk, ipi numak, e'wikwe'ctpe'nmukosie'k, onwaciwak cipam, wiasma cI ninwusimkIt.
40N||26||42||IcI minI e'ki macit, iw nishuk, ipi kinume'‘ otI kikito, O! Nose', kishpIn otI mnukwackIn wipwakwe'pmosankoian mnukwe'ian ie'k, kin e'shte'an knomkIt.
40N||26||43||IcI minI e'kipie'shiat okimkawan e'npanIt minI‘, osam e'kikipkoshwat.
40N||26||44||Okinknan cI e'kishiat minI e'kiwunumat, iw otI nsuk, nasap cI minI kiwukIto.
40N||26||45||IcI e'kipiat ni ke'knomowacIn otI cI okinan npak, ipi nwashmok, pInI, pe'shoc pie'mkIt, tpukIn icI We'kwIsmukot NInwun e'wiwie'shIt one'cinuk me'iashowe'psIncIn.
40N||26||46||Psukwik kInmamacimIn; pe'shoc iuwak wapataIt.
40N||26||47||Me'kwa cI e'iIt nankitok, pInI, Cwte's nkot ki mtatso shItInish e'tshIcIk, kipie' okipie'wice'okon ke'cmaoce'‘tinIt, e'pie' ionIt kishkonIn, ipi iaptuwunIn e'ocIpiawat kcIme'matmocuk onInimwan, ipi oke'ctaosimwan ki nIshInape'k.
40N||26||48||IcI o wawie'shat okiwitmowan washI kInwatInmawat, otI cI okinan. Osu ke'oce'muk, oie'o mackonuk.
40N||26||49||IcI win e'kipie'shiat e'ciiInIt ni CisusIn, icI otI okinan, KtInmukon Ke'knomakIn; icI e'kiwce'mat.
40N||26||50||Cisus cI otI okinan, Nikan, We'kwnicI pie'ocIshian? Kipie'shie'k cI ki kipie'm mackonawan ni CisusIn.
40N||26||51||IcI pInI, nkot kapmIwice'wakIn ni CisusIn, kishipnuke'no, icI, e'kiwtapnuk okishkowun, icI e'kiwe'potwat opmitakaimInIn ni kcI-me'matmot; icI e'kikishkitoke'shwat.
40N||26||52||OtI cI Cisus okinan, minI shiton i kishkowun kacIte'k ki caye'k ke'otapnukuk kishkowun; okupnacukwunawa i kishkowun.
40N||26||53||KtIshte'anI co ntakshkItosin e'wi nume'kituwuk Nos, kie'nup e'wi mishpI mtatso wusimI shItInish iaianke' maoce'tincIn mIshInwe'n?
40N||26||54||KishpIn otI oshIcke'ian, tInicI ke'ocI te'pwe'mkukipIn notI we'npie'kate'k? otI cI knomkIt.
40N||26||55||Iwpic cI Cisus okiknonan, ni maoce'tincIn kupie'otIsumnI, ke'cwa ke'mockIt e'pie'ioie'k kishkomwan, ipi kiaptuwInwIn e'wiwtapne'ie'k. Nkicipitup ca‘wi, pIne'‘ e'kInomonkon shi kcI-nume'okumkok cocI kimackonsim.
40N||26||56||Caye'k otI kishIckate'pIn e'te'pwe'mkuk nakanacimocuk kashupie'ke'wat. IcI ni caye'k ke'knomowacIn e'ki nkItnIshmukot;
40N||26||57||IcI ki kamackonawat ni CisusIn, okishonawan e'ciiInIt, Ke'ie'pusIn ni kcI- me'matmot onInI we'npie'ke'ncIn, ipi ke'ctaosIncIn e'she'maoce'tinIt.
40N||26||58||Pitu cI shkwe'iak okipmInashkawan, shi kcI-me'matmot onInI e'tanIt; icI e'kipitike't okiwitpuman pmitakaiIn e'wiwaptuk wakosanuk.
40N||26||59||KiwcI kcI-me'matmocuk o nInwuk ipi ke'ctaose'cuk, ipi caye'k kikitowun okipantawapmawan waknaoshke'mawacIn ni CisusIn e'wiwcInsawat cI.
40N||26||60||CocI wIiI okimkawasiwan, e'ki ianwI mane'nIt waknoshkImawacIn kipie'n, cocI okimkawasiwan, ici shkwe'iak kipie'k nish waknoshkImawacIn.
40N||26||61||OtI cI kikItwuk, OtIsI otI kikIto, NtakshkIton e'wipnactoian okIc nume'okumuk Kshe'mIne'to, icI ntakishton nsokwnukuk.
40N||26||62||IcI kcI-me'matot onInI, kipsukwi, otI cI okinan; ConI ke'ko kitIshnkwe'take'si? we'kwnicI, kotI e'shmukon.
40N||26||63||Cisus cI coke'ko kikItsi. OcI kcI-me'matwot onInI okinkwe'twan otI okinan: OsI pe'matsIt Ke'she'mIne'to, ntInap e'wiwitmoie'k, tanak kin Knayst We'kwIsmukwiIn Kshe'mIne'to.
40N||26||64||Cisus cI otI okinan, KikishkItsu. OtI win Nin KtInum; pama kuwapmawa We'kwIsmukot NInwun e'cipitupIt ote'pniwnak, iw okIshke'‘wsowun, ipi e'piat shi ankwotok shpumuk.
40N||26||65||IcI o kcI-me'matmot onInI, e'kinanisikpe'tot paskukIn: otI cI kikito, Pukon we'takwsI; we'kwnicI wusimI ke'ocI ntotwukon ki waiacimocuk pInI nawa kinotwawa e'pkonwutakwsIt. 
40N||26||66||TInicI e'shte'aie'k? okinkwe'twawancI otI cI kikItwuk? Ne'ntakwse'‘ sI e'winpot.
40N||26||67||IcI e'kiskowanawat w‘shkishkonuk, ipi okipkwakwnIcitwawan, ipi anIt okiwe'potwawan, onIciwan.
40N||26||68||OtI cI okinawan, nakanacimotwushnak, kin Knayst; We'nicI kawe'potakwiIn?
40N||26||69||OcI Pitu kicipitupI nkoci shi wikwamuk, icI she'shksiIn kipie'naskakon, otI cI okikon; Kinsuke' kipmI wice'wa Cisus o Ke'nIni onInI.
40N||26||70||Caye'k cI e'nasmukapwunIt kiakwne'tum, otI cI, okinan; Cokuke'nmIsnon e'kiton.
40N||26||71||IcI kanmusakuk, icI kanmiIt te'skanuk, pe'kansIncIn she'shksiIn okiwapmukon, otI cI okinan, shiw e'inIncIn, otI sI ke'win okipmI wice'wan ni CisusIn; Ne'sIni onInI.
40N||26||72||IcI minI e'ki iakwne'take't e'ki kie'tnamtakwsIt, CosI nkuke'nmasi onInI.
40N||26||73||IcI minI shkIc okipie'naskakon pe'mkapowIncIn, ipi okinawan ni PutuiIn,We'we'nI sI ke'kin, kapme'nashkuwut kuke'ntakwIs e'shumiIn knIstotakwIs.
40N||26||74||IcI e'we'p mIci kikitot, otI cI kikito, Cosu nkuke'nmasi onInI; IcI pic e'notakwsIt pkuakwa.
40N||26||75||Okimikwe'ntancI Pitu kakot, ni CisusIn, e'kikot e'pwamshinotakwsIt pku‘akwa, nsuk, coin nin nkuke'nmasi, kIshI. IcI e'kisakuk e'kiwukcumwut.
40N||27||1||PIC cI kawapuk, caye'k ki kcI-me'matmocIk onInwuk, ipi oke'ctaosiwmawan ki nIshInape'k, okItshImawan ni CisusIn e'winsawat.
40N||27||2||IcI katkopnawat okimacinawan, okipkItnumwawan, ni Pantus Payne'tun okuma.
40N||27||3||OcI Cwte's kapkIt e'nmat, kawapmat cI e'winsIckasnIt; kikisate'ntum, icI e'kipie'tot ne'iap i nswapituk tswapuk shonia okopie'twan ni kcIme'matmocuk onInwun, ipi ke'ctaosIncIn.
40N||27||4||OtI cI okinan, Nkukie'patIs e'ki pkIte'ntuman pwamiashtotumomkuk mskwI. OtI cI kItwuk, We'kwnicI ninan i? Kin sI i mtIno.
40N||27||5||IcI mcIiukwan e'kipukitot, i shonia shi kcIe'nume'okumkok, icI e'ki macit e'ki wukontIsot.
40N||27||6||IcI ki kcI-me'matmocIk onInwuk okiwtapnumwat i shonia, otI cI kItwuk, CotawunsInon, e'witoikon maocIcke'wunuk, osam otI kakshkIcke'k mskwI.
40N||27||7||Ki kikitokcI icI kitawe'kcI ni shoniaiIn kikishpIne'twawancI wapukIn naknukI onInI okshtkan, e'winkowawat me'mataosIncIn.
40N||27||8||Ie'i we'tshInkate'k MskwI ktukan, otI e'kishkiwuk.
40N||27||9||Ie'i te'pwe'wunukuk kakitot CinImayi Nakanacimot otI kItwak, okiwtapnanawa i nswapituk nswapuk shonia, kapite'ntakwsIt o kipInoce'iuk Isniuk kapite'nmawat.
40N||27||10||OkominawancI i onaknukI onInI ashkIot ce'i okItkanI kanakwnIt Kshe'mIne'to.
40N||27||11||IcI Cisus e'kinipwIt e'nasmupnIt niw okuma, icI o okuma e'natowat otI cI otInan, Kin, ni kitokumaomukok ki Cwiuk? IcI Cisus, otI otInan kitukItsI.
40N||27||12||Pic cI kianmikakot ni kcI-me'matmocuk onInwun, ipi ke'ctaosIncIn; coke' ki okishInkwe'‘twasin.
40N||27||13||OtI cI Payne't, okinan, conI kinotsin me'kwe'tso ke'ko e'shIi miane'nmukon?
40N||27||14||ConI tIna nkotuk okiknonasin; kikcI mamkate'ntum cI o okuma.
40N||27||15||IwcI e'wikwtuk, okume' kakuk okipkIte'man nkote'ie' ke'pakwukasnIt ke'wawinanIt ni nIshInape'n.
40N||27||16||Oki iu wawancI ke'ke'ntakwse'nIt kie'pakwukasnIt Pane'pe's shInkaswun.
40N||27||17||IcI pic kamaoce'tiwat Payne't, otI okinan We''nicI ne'twe'nme'k e'wipkItnumon kon; Pe'ne'pe's tanake' Cisus e'shnukasot Knayst?
40N||27||18||E'ke'nmat ni e'kakiawe'nmanIt kaocI pkItnumakot.
40N||27||19||Pic cI kacipitupIt shi tupaknukI pItie'pwunuk, wiwun kipie' mcIcimokie'n otI cI kikItwun; Ke'ko nkot totwakIn one'pwakatnInI; kcImce'sh ke'ko win we'cwitaiapituman nkom e'kishkiwuk.
40N||27||20||KicI kcI-me'matmocuk onInwuk, ipi ke'ctaose'cuk okiwishte'pmawan ni maoce'tincIn e'wi ntotma ke'nIt Pane'pe'sIn; nicI e'winshonacumIt CisusIn.
40N||27||21||IcI okuma okinkwe'twan, otI cI okinan, We'nicI nkote'ie' ki kiIpkItnumonkon; OtI cI kikItwuk, Pane'pe's.
40N||27||22||Payne't cI otI okinan. TInicI ke'totwuk Cisus e'shnukasot Knayst. OtI cI caye'k okikon nocma win KIskakwukaso.
40N||27||23||IcI okuma kikIto, Taci? We'konicI kamcItotuk? WusimI cI kiwishkowe'k, otI cI kikItwuk, Nocma win KIskakwukaso.
40N||27||24||Pic cI Payne't e'waptuk ke'ko e'wipwakshkItot, wusimI na‘wuc e'nshkatsInIt, okiwtapinan mpish, icI e'ki ksincat e'nasmukapwunIt maoce'tincIn, otI cI kikIto, Coin nin nsikwe'pnumwasi ne'pwakat omuskwim; Kinwa wi ke'shuwe'psowe'kwe'n.
40N||27||25||Caye'k cI ki nIshInape'k okinkwe'twawan, otI cI kikItwuk, Nocma ninan nkupukitakomIn iw mIskwim kIte'nI, ipi nicanse'nanuk.
40N||27||26||IcI e'kipkItnumwat ni Pane'pe'sIn, icI ni CisusIn, kapsItie'wat okipkItnan e'wiskakwukasnIt.
40N||27||27||IcI ni otI shumakunIshimIn okuma, okimacinawan ni CisusIn kikitokumkok, icI e'kipie'naskakot caye'k shumakunIshIn e'tshInIt.
40N||27||28||OkiskotnawancI icI e'kipiskotnawat mskwe'kIn kwawun.
40N||27||29||Pic cI kakate'nmowat sisokwe'psowun, cukunukaoshisun okitawawan otupik, ipi nasaknIshk okitawan ote'pne'cik, icI e'kiw wucik kwuItwawat e'nasmupkapwunIt, icI okinapitotwawan,, otI cI okinawan, We'we'nI‘ we'kuma omukwiIn Cwiuk.
40N||27||30||IcI e'ki skowanawat, ipi kiw tapnanawa i nasakunIshk, icI e'kiwe'potwawat otupik.
40N||27||31||KashkIc napitotwawat okikiskotnawan, icI win kapiskuk kipiskotnawan, icI e'kishonawat e'wiskakwawat.
40N||27||32||Kapie'sakumwat cI ikiwapmawan, Se'nini nInwun Sayiman e'shInkaswun; niw cI kitwe' okinawan e'wipmotonIt ni iashte'iatkomnIn.
40N||27||33||Pic ci kanmupiawat e'shnukate'k, KanIkate', i e'tmuk O Knatup e'cite'k.
40N||27||34||Okimanawan Siwapo, ipi wisup, katkostowat e'wiminukwe'nIt; icI kakwucupituk, co ki mnukwe'sin.
40N||27||35||IcI e'kiskakwawat, ipi okiswe'nmowawan kapiskumnIt icI e'kitatiwat e'wite'pwe'wunukuk kakitot Nakanacimot, okiswe'nawan paskamInIn e'tshawat, ipi npiskumwakIn kaocI tatiwat.
40N||27||36||Kicipitupwuk cI otukwapmawan cIshi.
40N||27||37||IcI e'kitowawat shiw otupik we'npie'kate'nuk we'cawat, OTI CISUS OTOKUMAMWAN KI CWIUK.
40N||27||38||Ipi cI nish kie'motshke'cuk, kitko Skakwukaswuk; nkot ote'pniwnak, nkot cI o onumciwnak.
40N||27||39||KicI kapmose'cuk ikikuke'cawan e'mumukwe'twawat.
40N||27||40||OtI cI otInawan, Kin, pe'nactin kcInume'okumuk, ipi kashIton e'nsokwnukuk ke'skontIson. KishpIn okwIsmukwiIn Kshe'mIne'to, pie'nisasin shi kiashte'iakwukinuk.
40N||27||41||Winwa ke'ki kcIme'matmocIk onInwuk okinatkoawan, kike' onupie'ke' onInwuk, ipi ke'ctaose'cuk okinawan.
40N||27||42||Pe'kansIncIn cI okike'skonan, win cI co ke'skontusi. KishpIn sI we'tokmaomukwe'n IsniIn, nocma win Kom kupie'nisasi shi ashte'atkok icI ke'cI te'pwe'twukon.
40N||27||43||Okipe'nmonIn Kshe'mIne'ton, nocma win oka‘tapne'kin, kishpIn waiaokokwe'n, otI kakItot Nin NtokwIsmuk Kshe'mIne'to.
40N||27||44||KicI ke'mockicuk katukwakwukascuk win wa ke'i kanawat.
40N||27||45||Nawkwe'k cI kikiskupkonia, e'nkokwukumkiak ukI; nash nsotupukIn e'pite'ntakwuk.
40N||27||46||Pic cI nso tupukInuk Cisus kikcInotakwse'wak, otI cI kItwak, Inay, Inay, ne'me' se'pe'kte'nay? otI e'kitok, Nkishe'mIne'tom Nkishe'mIne'tom, We'kwnicI we'c nkIshiun?
40N||27||47||KicI anIt shikanipwoe'cuk pic i kanotmowat, kikItwuk; OtI nInI onItuman Inaisun.
40N||27||48||Kie'nup cI nkot kimace'pto, icI e'kiw tapnuk Skuapowan, kiwumoshkIne'tot siwapo, icI e'kitot, e'kinapsItot shi nasakunIshkok okiminancI, e'wimnukwe'nIt.
40N||27||49||KicI anIt otI kikItwuk, Ponuk, nocma wapmatan kI‘nwa ok?pie'skonkon ni Inaisun.
40N||27||50||Cisus cI kanotakwsIt minI e'pic kotakuk, okipkItnan ocipamIn.
40N||27||51||PInI iwcI kaiakwukote'k, pic iukwan kcInume'okumkok, shpumuk kipie'ocIpikw‘shke' nashcI mtukumuk; ipi kI‘ kimacke'mkIt ipi ni sInie'n kipaskukie'ton.
40N||27||52||Ipi kinsakshke'ton ni cipe'okumkwe'n, mce'sh cI kanpacuk kanumawakupIne'n, kiwnIshke'mkItnI wiwuwan;
40N||27||53||Kipie' ocI sakumwuk shi cipe'‘okumkok, kakishiapsinIt, kipitike'kcI kcI-otanuk mce'sh cI okiwaptuawan wiwuwan.
40N||27||54||Pic cI Kapte'n, ipi ni kapmI wice'okocIn, kakowapmacIk CisusIn, e'waptumwat kI e'nanimshkanuk, ipi kanomkItInuk kikcIse'ksik; otI cI kikItwuk, We'we'ne'sI otI okiwkwIsmukon Kshe'mIne'ton.
40N||27||55||Kimane'k ke'shi kwe'k, pnoc e'wsapmawat kapie'pmnashkawacuk CisusIn kiw cupie'k Ke'nInIuk, e'wipmitwawat.
40N||27||56||Winke' shi kitkoie' Me'ni Me'kte'ne'n, ipi Me'niIn, kaokie'macIn Ce'ms, ipi Cosus, ipi okie'iwan Se'piti onicansIn.
40N||27||57||Pic cI e'nmupkonianuk kipie' ocupie' E'nIme'tiuk ke'c tpe'nwe'osIt nInI, Cosip kishInkaso, win kie' Cisus kaknomakot.
40N||27||58||IcI tkishiat Paye'ntIn, e'kiwuntotmowat Cisus wiwuwIn. IcI Paye'nt cI kikito, e'wipkItumwut i wiia‘w.
40N||27||59||IcI Cosip kaotapnuk i wiia‘w okiwikwe'ie'kinan wapshkie'kIn pukwoian, panakwtInuk.
40N||27||60||OkiwusancI tpInwe' otoshkicipe'okumkok kawe'napkaumatsokupIne'n, shi sInik; icI e'ki tupce'nuk kcI-sIn, e'shkwate'mwunuk, icipe'okumkok, icI e'kinke'tuk.
40N||27||61||Kiie' cI shi Me'ni Me'kte'ne'n, ipi o pe'kansIt Me'ni, kicipitukwuk cI ashowe'iukwan shi cipe'‘okumkok.
40N||27||62||Ka WiiapukcI kakish oshIstowat i mkoshe'wun; ki kcI me'matmocIk onInwuk, ipi Pe'nisiuk kipie' wice'twuk, Payne'tIn kipie' shie'k;
40N||27||63||OtI cI ikinawan Okuma, nmikwe'ntamIn kakItpIt okawie'shke'mot me'kwa e'ie' pmatsIt; Kinsokwnukuk nkaonIshka minI.
40N||27||64||KIton e'wikawapcikate'k nash i nsokishuk i cipe'‘oknmuk; tanupie'n ke'knomowacIn e'ie'pko nianuk e'wikimocwunkot; otI cI Otanawan ni nIshInape'n, KipsukwiwaksI e'npopI iwcI i ne'tum.
40N||27||65||Paye'nt cI otI okinan, anwusI KtIiwawak e'kwapicuk; ktashiamsI wawishkItok tso ke'kshkItoie'k.
40N||27||66||IcI e'ki shiawat e'ki wa‘wishkItowat i cipe'okumuk, e'ki tkwapkIstowat i sIn, ipi okisawan e'kwapInIt.
40N||28||1||KAPONUM e'kishkuk e'pie'wasapuk i ne'tum e'kishkiwuk wik, kipie'shiI Me'ni Me'ktIne'n, ipi o pe'kansIt Me'ni, e'pie'waptumwat cipe'‘ okumuk.
40N||28||2||IcI pInI, e'ki kcImackanuk kI; Kshe'mIne'to omIshIne'we'mIn shpumuk kipie' ocupie'n, icI e'kipiat nkoci cI okine'nan i sIn kakpakwuke'k shi shkwate'muk icI e'ki kwuctiie'pIt.
40N||28||3||E'shnakwsItcI ke'cwa e'wawasmok, ipi paskuk kiwapshkianI ke'cwakon.
40N||28||4||E'pic kwsawat cI kikakowapcuk kinukshke'k, ipi ne'pkIn kishowe'psik.
40N||28||5||OcI mshInwe' okinkwe'twan, otI okinan nikwe'n ke'ko kwtacke'k; kuke'nme'num Cisus e'ntuwapme'k, kaskakukwasot.
40N||28||6||Cowi shotI ie'si; kiw nIshke'wak, kakItpIt, Piak pie'waptumok kacIshkIshuk, Te'pe'nke't.
40N||28||7||Kie'nup shiak ipi kuitmowawak, ke'knomowacIn e'kiwnIshkanIt e'npopIt; pInI, nmInikani cawin ipI Ke'ne'niuk shiw ie'shi ke'cI wapme'k, pInI, kikiwitmonum.
40N||28||8||IcI e'kin mamaciwat e'ki nkItmowat kie'nup, i cipe'‘okumuk kikwtacwuk, ipi kinciwe'n- mok; icI kipmupitok e'wiwitmowawat ke'knomowancIn.
40N||28||9||IcI e'nmamaciwat e'wuwitmowawat ni ke'knomowancIn pInI, Cisus okinkwe'shkwan otI cI okinan; MnIwankosuk kinwa. IcI e'ki pmumackonawat osItinuk, ipi okiwucikwnItwawan.
40N||28||10||Cisus cI otI okinan; Ke'ko kwtacke'k wuwitmowuk nikane'iuk e'wishiawat Ke'nIniuk shiw ke'cI wapmowat.
40N||28||11||Me'kwacI e'nmIpiskawat, pInI anIt e'kwapcIkipie'shie'k kcI otanuk, icI e'kiwitmowawat kcI.me'matmocIk onInwun, cake'ko kashowe'puk.
40N||28||12||Pic cI kamaoce'tiwat, ipi niw ke'ctaose'cIk ki-kikitot okiminawan mce'sh shonia ni shumaknushIn;
40N||28||13||OtI cI okinawan, otI kItok, ke'knomowacIn kipie'nme'kwa e'pkoniaiuk kipie'kimocwunkon, e'ie' npaiak.
40N||28||14||KishpIn cI otI, notuk okuma, nkuwishte'pmamIn, icI ke'cI pkIte'nmukwie'k.
40N||28||15||Okwtapnanawa cI i shonia kitotmokcI kanItwa; icI ie'i ke'iapI e'kitowat ki Cwiuk nash otI e'kishciwuk.
40N||28||16||IcI ki mtatso shItnkot ke'knomowacIn kishumacin shi Ke'ne'niuk kishie'k e'shpItnianuk kacI wawitmakwat ni CisusIn.
40N||28||17||IcI kawapmawat okiw wucikwnItwawan, anIt cI kiianwe'ntumwuk.
40N||28||18||Cisus cI okipie' knonan otIcI okinan, Caye'k kshke'‘e'‘osuwun nminko, ipI shpumuk kishkok, ipi shotI kik.
40N||28||19||WimaciksI knomouk caye'k e'tso ikIswat nIshInape'k; kcItapie'nuk otInoswunuk o We'osmIt, ipi o We'kwIsmIt ipi o KcI Ocipam.
40N||28||20||Ke'nomouk e'wi te'pwe'tmowat cak ke'ko kashI ke'kmInkon; PInI kakuksI kowice'wInum nash wishkwakiwuk. E'me'n.
44N||1||1||NKIWSHITON ne'tum msInukIn, O Tiapinus, caye'k Cisus kaoshkawe'pwshItot, ipi e'ki kuknomake't.
44N||1||2||Nash i e'kishkIwuk kaotapnukasot, shpumuk kakishminat okukie'kwe'wunIn shi PanakwsIt Cipam, ni nwakanacIn kaowe'napmacIn;
44N||1||3||Nie'ni ke'iapI kawaptacIn wia’w e'pmatsIt kakish kwtukitot shi mce'sh we'we'nI te'pwe'tatwunIn e'kiwapmukot nie'waptuk tsokwun ipi e'kiactuk cake'ko Kshe'mIne'to otokumauwunuk:
44N||1||4||Me'kwacI e'ie' maosomat okiwitmowan e'wipwa shi ocI macinIt Cinose'ne'muk e'wi pwitowat Osma kowawituk, win kakitot nin kaocI notake'ie'k.
44N||1||5||Can we'we'nI ki kcItapie'nwe', mpik nIshcI kinwa kukcItapie'nkom, shi panakwsIt Cipam e'pwamshI mce'shkonkuk. 
44N||1||6||IcI kamaoce'tiwat okinatawawan otI kikItwuk Te'pe'nke'n ConI otI e'picak minI kuminasi Isne'iIn o kumauwun.
44N||1||7||IcI otI okinan cosu wi kinwa e'wi ke'ntume'k pic nikan wapiamkuk win osma katot shi owishkIswunuk.
44N||1||8||KuotItnanawa wishkIswun ipi panakwsIt Cipam kikishotIskoie'k, ipi nin kaocI witmake'm caye'k shi Cinose'ne'muk ipi caye'k Cwtie'uk, ipi shi Se'me'ne'ok ipi shi mamwI pnocak shotI kik.
44N||1||9||Pic cI kakish iactuk notI ke'ko me'kwa e'ie' wapmawat kiwcI otapnIkaso shpumuk; ipi shi ankoton okipon wapmawan.
44N||1||10||Me'kwacI e'ie' kanapwat ipI shpumuk; kanmIshianIt, pInI nish nInwun okiwicka pwutakwan kiwapshkianI kapiskumwacIn.
44N||1||11||OtI cI ke'iapI okikowan, Ke'nIni tshI nInituk tacI we'cnipwoie'k shpumuk e'napie'k? OtI nasap Cisus, kaocI otapnImakoie'k shpumuk; iw nasap ke'shI piat kashu wapme'k shpumuk kashu shiat.
44N||1||12||IcI Cinose'ne'muk kishu kiwe'k kiwcIpie'k e'pkotnianuk AnIpIt kishInkate' e'nume'kishkuk e'picak shi Cinose'ne'muk.
44N||1||13||Pic cI kapitke'we't shpumuk kishie'k wikwamuk kaci iuwat Pitu, ipi Ce'ms, ipi can ipi E'ntnu, Pinip, ipi Tame's, Pe'toniu, ipi Me'to ‘Ce'ms kaokwIsmukot E'npiusIn, ipi Sayi mun Sinotus, ipi Cwte's, wikane'iIn Ce'ms.
44N||1||14||KotI caye'k pIne' kimsone'ntumwuk akimimawat, ipi kimumatmok shi kiInkwe'n, ipi Me'ni kaokie'imat o Cisus ipi niw wikane'iIn
44N||1||15||IwcI notI e'kishkiwuk Pitu KinipwI na‘iukwan ni ke'knomake'cuk (e'tshuwat cukI tInoswunwa kansoiwat nkotwaktshik, ipi nishwaptuk) otI cI kikIto;
44N||1||16||NInituk, ipi nikane'ituk, otI kikItowIn taocI nomkuk e'wite'pwe'mkuk Te'pIt kaocI kItot ni PanakwsIncIn CipamIn e'kiiacimat nikan ni Cwte'sIn, win kapmInikansIt e'kiwtapnawat CisusIn.
44N||1||17||Win kiwictkokcIkaso ipi o kiwtItnan anIt otI pmitake'wun
44N||1||18||OtI nInI okikishpIne'ton ktukan iwtpu‘ ukoswun miashuwe'psiwun, ipi nikan kishI pmokocIn kitokce'shInce' na‘iukwan icI caye'k picnI kisaktakwte'nI.
44N||1||19||Ipi otI okikuke'ntanawa, caye'k ki katacuk shi Cinose'ne'muk kikuke'ncIkate' i ktukan, e'shInkate'kw winwa kwiuk e'shumwat E'sIntime' e'tmuk i ktukan mskwI.
44N||1||20||Osam onIpie'kate' shi msInukIn Nkumwunuk, Win e'tat kupe'pshukwsInI ipi cowIiI shi Ite'si, ipi i otukwapke'wun pe'kansInIt okinapshkamakon.
44N||1||21||OtI cI ie'i kotI nInwuk kapmuwice'okonuk, pIne' Tope'nmukwiIkon Cisus e'ki pitike't, ipi e'kisakuk, shi e'cIiIikon.
44N||1||22||E'we'pkcItapie'nwe't Can nash i e'kishkiwuk kaotapnmakoikon nkot okInapshkawan e'wi wicwitma ke'ikon e'ki iapsishnInIt.
44N||1||23||Okiwe'napmawan cI Nish Cosip kishInkaso Pe'se'pe's ipi ke'iapI kashInkasot Custus, ipi Me'taye's.
44N||1||24||IcI e'kinumawat, ipi otI kikItwuk; Kin Te'pe'nke'n, kin ke'ke'ntumwutwa, caye'k nInwuk ote'‘iwan, knomoshInak we'kwe'nshutuk kote' nkote'iI kaowe'napmItwa.
44N||1||25||Win e'wi anIt pmitake't ipi NokantawIn win o Cwte's kaocI pmukocIk iw omaia tuwe'psiwun, win e'wishiat tpInowe' e'cIiIt.
44N||1||26||IcI e'kitatiwat wincI Me'taye's kiw tapnuk aso ipi kitkokcIkaso ni mtatso shItnkot nwakanmIcIn.
44N||2||1||Pic e'kishkuk PIntikast wikwtowun kaocItsak, caye'k kimsote'e'k kimaoce'‘tik mamwInkoci.
44N||2||2||IcI ka‘w kiwcI pie'mkItnI notakwsIwun shpumuk ke'cwa e'ki cI wishkanmuk, ipi kimosh kIne'se'nI caye'k shi wikwamuk kacI cipitupwat.
44N||2||3||Owaptanawa se'knInwaknIn ne'swakwianuk ke'cwa shkote', ipi nankot e'tshowat kite'nI wiwuwak.
44N||2||4||Ipi caye'k okimoshkIne'shkakwan ni PankwsIt Cipam icI kiwe'pkakikitok pkan kinowe'k kashu minkowat OcipamIn.
44N||2||5||Kite'kcI ipI CInose'ne'muk Cwiuk me'noshuwe'pse'cuk nInwuk e'tsoshumowat shotI kik kiwcIpie'k mtunmuk shpumuk.
44N||2||6||IcI otI kanotmoat, pnoc kamaoce'ticutk kipie'maoke'tik? ipi kimamkate'ntumwut os am e'tshIt nInI okinotwawan e'kikitonIte'shumot.
44N||2||7||Caye'kcI kimamkate'ntumwuk, ipi pkan okine'mawan otIcI kishItwuk, PInI coe'I kotI caye'k kakitocuk Ke'nIni nInwuk?
44N||2||8||TInicI e'shnotwukon e'tshIt nInI, e'ki ie'i nowe'ikon kashu nikiiIkon.
44N||2||9||Pe'tie'nuk, ipi Mitiuk, ine'mituk ipi ki e'tacuk shi MIsopote'miuk, ipi shi Cwtie'uk, Kpe'toshie'uk shi Pantusuk ipi E'shie'uuk,
44N||2||10||Pnicie'uk ipi shi e'kiwuk Nipie'uk ipi ipI Sinie'nk ipi pwake'ntakwse'cuk kiw cupie'k Nom ipi Cwiuk ipi te'pwe' twacIk.
44N||2||11||E'nitniuk, ipi E'ne'pie'niuk knotwamIn e'kikitowat e'shumie'kon o oimamkate'nta kwIwun Kshe'mIne'ton.
44N||2||12||Ipi caye'k ki mamkate'ntumwuk ipi kikwinwune'ntumwuk otIcI kishItwuk, we'kwnicI otI we'cnom Kuk?
44N||2||13||AnItcI okinaptotwawan kItwuk, kotIsI nInwuk Omoshkne'shkakwnawa wshkI shomnapo.
44N||2||14||NIshcI Pitu akiwickapwutwan ni mtatso shItnkot okiknonan otI okinan; kinwa e'tshI nIniwie'k Cwtie'uk, ipi caye'k kinwa, e'taie'k Cinose'ne'muk otI kuke'ntmok, ipi psItumok notI nkikitoonIn,
44N||2||15||Cowi kotI kiwIshkwe'pie'sik i e'ne'nme'k o samkIni nsotpukIn e'kwokishkiwuk.
44N||2||16||OtIsi ie'i katuk nakanacimot Cowun; 
44N||2||17||OtI ke'nomkuk pic wishkwakishkiwuk kItwak Kshe'mIne'to NkIsikna ncipam kwIciukwan caye'k wias, ipi kokwIswak, ipi kitansu’wak knikanacimok, ipi ktoshInunwe'mwak kukwsaptumwuk ipi ktukwe'simawak oke'iapwatanawa iapwe'wunIn.
44N||2||18||Ipi npumitakaimuk, ipi ntupa’nkwe'imuk nkIsiknumwak ncipamIn niw e'kishkiwuk icI knikanacimok.
44N||2||19||Ipi nkuwaptuwe' mamkate'ntumwunIn shi shpumuk kishkok, ipi mataoshuwe'psuwun shotI kik namiukwan, mskwI, ipi shkote', ipi ke'c pkwe'ne'k.
44N||2||20||Ipi kisIs kukiskupkoniawapkIse', ipi tpukisIs kumskwiwe' e'pwamshupiamkuk i kcIkishIk, ipi omiuk kukishkom Kshe'mIne'to.
44N||2||21||KnomkItcI we'kwe'ntuk ke'wawitmowakwe'n otInoswun Kshe'mIne'to kuke'skona.
44N||2||22||Isne'iuk e'tshI nIniwie'k psItmok notI kikitonIn Cisus Ne'sInI nInI kamnonwe'kot Kshe'mIne'to kamataototuk, ipi mamkate'ntumwunIn, ipi mataoshuwe'psuwunIn win Kshe'mIne'to katotuk shi wiwunuk me'kwe' nawe'nI kinwa ke'iapI kuke'ntanawa.
44N||2||23||Win kapkItnukasot kane'nmat ipi nikan kashuke'nmat Kshe'mIne'to, kinwa kautapne'k ipi kmIconIciwan kiskakwawa ipi kinsawa.
44N||2||24||Win Kshe'mIne'to kapsukwitmat kaiapskopitot, i wis ke'ntumwun shi upomuk, o samco otakshkumac konkosin shiw.
44N||2||25||Osam Te'pIt otI kItwak e'ki iacimot, nikan nkiwapma Kshe'mIne'to pIne'’ e'nasmupian shiuwak nte'pniw nak, e'wi pwamatpe'ian.
44N||2||26||IwcI ie'i nte'’ kimnowankosimkIt ipi nse'knInwakIn kinciwe'nmomkIt wusimI ke'iapI ntuwiasum kInwashmomkIt shi pkose'nmowunuk.
44N||2||27||Osam kin, cokInkinasi ncipam shi namkumuk, coke'kin kIne'nmasi panakwsIt Nkot e'wiwaptuk mpIshknInwun.
44N||2||28||KikInomowasha pmatse'ian kin kumoshkIne'sto’w papine'nmowun shi ktIshnakwsiwunuk.
44N||2||29||NInituk ipi nikane'ituk nocima we'we'nI kuknonum e'witshumuk, o osma Te'pIt iw e'kinpot, ipi e'kinkokasot, ipi i ocipe'okumuk e'ci iIikon te'nI otI e'kishkiwuk.
44N||2||30||Osam win e'iacimot ipi e'ke'ntuk Kshe'mIne'ton e'kie'tnamukot niw nicansun shiw otowiasmuk okaocI psukwitnan ni KnaystIn e'wi cipitupnIt shiw cipitupwunuk.
44N||2||31||Win nikane'kiwaptuk okitshItomowan e'wiapsishnInIt ni KnaystIn nike', ocipamIn, cokinkIc kasin shi namkumuk coke'i otowiasum co kiwaptusin mpIshknInwun.
44N||2||32||OtI Cisus Kshe'mIne'to kapsukwitnat ie'i kinan caye'k watmake'ikon.
44N||2||33||Iw ie'i ote'pniwnanuk Kshe'mIne'ton kapsukwitnukot ipi kaminkoni osIn kawawitmakot ni panakwsIncIn CipamIn kanitawe't iw nkom waptume'k ipi nwatme'k.
44N||2||34||Osam Te'pIt comshu shpumuk shiIsi nIshcI. win tpInwe' kIto, Te'pe'nke't okinan ni Te'pe'n mukwian, cipitupIn shotI nte'pniwnak.
44N||2||35||Nash kiw shu ukwa me'iane'nmukwiIn e'wipIste'piIn.
44N||2||36||OtI cI ie'i caye'k otu wikwamwa Isne'iIn we'we'nI okuke'ntana Kshe'mIne'to okiwshuan oie'o Cisus kinwa kaskakwoe'k ne'ne'ish Te'pe'nke't ipi Knayst.
44N||2||37||Pic cI otI kanotmoat kiptukte'e'shke'k ipi otI okinawan ni PituIn, ipi ni anIt nwakanmIcIn NInituk ipi nikane'ituk we'kwnicI ke'totmukon.
44N||2||38||OtI cI Pitu okinan kisate'ntmok, ipi kcItapie'nkasok e'tshIie'k shiw tInoswunuk Cisus Knayst e'wi we'pnakoie'k ni kmIiashuwe'psiwnawan icI kuminkom i mikwe'wun o panakwsIt Cipam.
44N||2||39||Osam i wawitmake'wun, kuwawitmakom, ipi ki ktupInoce'imowak ipi ki caye'k pnoc e'icIk; ke'iapI tso Te'pe'nke't Kshe'mIne'tomnan ke'ntomakwe'n.
44N||2||40||Ipi mce'sh pe'kankInkItwunIn, kiwitmake', ipi kikie'kwe', otI kikIto, kiskontIsok, shiw ki me'iashuwe'pse'cIk pmats cIk.
44N||2||41||Pic cI i kanciwe'nmocuk e'kiwtapnumwawat, iw kikitowun, kikcItapie'nkaswuk icI i e'kishkiwuk, nsuk mtatswak knIpIc kitshik.
44N||2||42||IcI kitotmok we'we'nI i nwakancuk ote'pwe'ie'ntumwunwa, ipi tpantuwun, ipi e'kipikupitowat pkwe'shkIn ipi e'numawat.
44N||2||43||Ipi se'ksowun, okiwtuskonawa e'tshuwat cipamwan, ipi mce'sh mamkate'ntumwunIn, ipi mataototmonIn kitotmok ki nwakancuk.
44N||2||44||Ipi caye'k ki te'pwe'ie'ntukuk mamwI kiik; otIpInoe'wsiwnawa mamawI okitupe'ne'ntanawa.
44N||2||45||Ipi kitawe'k otIpnoe'usiwnawan, ipi otInkackInwan, icI e'ki swe'nmowawat, caye'k nInwun kashumne'snIt cak nInwun.
44N||2||46||Ipi pIne'‘ e'tso kishkItnuk e'kimsone'ntumwuk shi kcI nume'okumkok ipi okipikupitonawa pkwe'shkIn, e'tsunuk wikwame'n ipi okimicnawa micum shi mnowankoswunuk, ipi kinkotnInI ote'‘iwa.
44N||2||47||E'winwanawat Kshe'mIne'ton, ipi e'mnonwe'awat caye'k nIshInape'n, ipi Kshe'mIne'to okiianke'san ni te'pwe'ie'ntumnIcIn e'tsokiskItnuk; ki wake'skonkascuk.
44N||3||1||IcI Pitu ipi Can, kiwice'twuk shpumuk kcI-nume'okumkok shaktso tpukIn e'pite'ntakwuk, pic wanumak.
44N||3||2||IwcI ukot nInI e'konikIt co kinupmose'si kipmaocIkaso; okisawan e'tso kishkuk e'cI shkwate'mkate'nuk kcI-nume'okumuk e'shnukate'k Ke'cwunuk; e'wintotmowawat mikwe'wunIn nipatike'nIt shi kcI-nume'okumkok.
44N||3||3||E'wapmatcI Pitu, ipi CanIn e'nmupitike'nut kcI-nume'okumkok okintotmowan mikwe'wun.
44N||3||4||Pitu cI okikanapman, ipi Can kItwak, WapmIshnak;
44N||3||5||IwcI okinaksowapman e'pkose'nmat ke'koe'wiminkot.
44N||3||6||Pitu cI kIto; Lonia ipi osaw shonia, cointe'isin; nIshcI e'toian kuminIn, Otnoswunuk, Cisus Knayst, Ne'se'nIt nInI, psukwin, ipi pmose'n.
44N||3||7||IwcI e'kiskInce'nat ote'pniciwnuk ipi okipsukwitnan iwcI papuk niwsIte'n ipi okate'n kiwishksimkItnI.
44N||3||8||IwcI e'kipsukwit kinipwI, ipi kipmose', ipi e'nmowice'wat shi kcI-nume'okumkok, e'nmupmose't, ipi e'nmukwakwaskwse'ot, ipi e'uwinwanat Kshe'mIne'ton.
44N||3||9||Ipi caye'k ki nIshInape'k oki wapmawan e'pmose'nIt, ipi e'uwinwananIt Kshe'mIne'ton.
44N||3||10||Okikike'nmawancI e'ki cipitupnIt shi ke'c wuntInuk shkwate'muk kcI-nume'okumkok icI kimoshkne'shkakwnawa kimamkate'ntumwun ipi okimamkate'nmawan kashu shuwe'ntakwsInIt.
44N||3||11||IwcI o pwanupmose't nInI kane'se'e't okimackonan PituIn ipi CanIn, caye'k ki cIshInape'k ki pItok e'ciInIt shkwate'muk e'shnukate'k Sanuman, otIshkwate'mwun kcImamkate'ntumwan.
44N||3||12||IwcI pic Pitu kawaptuk, okiknonan ni nIshInape'n, Kinwa isne'iuk nInwuk, we'kw nicI we'cmamkate'ntume'k otI ipi we'kwni, we'ckanapmiak, ke'cwa ninan te'pinak nwishkIsiwnInan tanke', nmInoshuwe'psiw nInan kaocIkshkukIt otI nInI e'wipmose't.
44N||3||13||Okshe'mIne'tomIn. E'pe'ne'e'm, ipi Aysik, ipi Ce'kap, ipi okshe'mIne'tomwan kosnanuk oki kcI pite'nman okwIsIm CisusIn kinwa kapkIte'n me'k, ipi kaian we'nme'k e'nasmupIt Payne't, pic kawishte'pwe't e'wipkItnat.
44N||3||14||NIshcI kianwe'nmawa panakwsIt, Nkot ipi me'noshuwe'psIt, iwcI kintuwe'nmawa e'wipkIte'ntmakoie'k.
44N||3||15||Okanshuwe't kintonawa okuma pmatsowun Kshe'mInato kapsukwItnuk shi npoonuk ninan iwe'cwitmake'iak
44N||3||16||Ipi otInoswunuk, ote'pwe'ie'ntumwIn shiw otInoswunuk, kaocI oshe'It otI nInI e'wishkIsIt kowapmawa ipi kuke'ntanaw we'we'nI ote'pwe'ie'ntumwun shiw tInosunuk we'cminIt otI kwiuk we'cne'se'e't e'nasmupie'k kinwa caye'k.
44N||3||17||Ipi nkom nikane'ituk, Nin kuke'ntan, ke'ko e'pwakuke'ntume'k iw, kaocItotme'k katotmowat ke'ki ktokmamwak.
44N||3||18||NIshcI notI cIie'k Kshe'mIne'to nikan kashu knomowat ni caye'k NakanacmoncIn, ni KnaystIn e'wikwutuke'ntumnIt, iwsI kanomkItnuk.
44N||3||19||Kisate'ntumok, ipi kwe'knoik tanakmIcshuwe'psiwnawan ktakasipie'makom, pic piamkuk e'wshkinakwutot e'nasmupIt Kshe'mIne'to.
44N||3||20||Cisus KnaystIn, okupie'nokanan ke'isha kashupie'wawitmakoie'k.
44N||3||21||Kishuk win, ke'otapnukot nash kiwcItsunuk cake'ko, win Kshe'mIne'to, kashI kikitot shiw toninuk caye'k panakwsIncIn Nakan acimoncIn nash e'kowe'pkiwuk
44N||3||22||Mosis we'we'nI okinan nosnanIn Nakan acimot Kshe'mIne'to Se'pe'nmukwie'k, kupsukwit namakwa kikane'iwak ke'cwa nin, winsu kupsItwawa cake'ko, we'kwe'ntuk ke'koie'k.
44N||3||23||KnomkItcI we'kwe'ntuk cipam ke'pwapsItwakwe'n ni nakanacimocIn win kupinatsI me'kwe' nIshnape'kI.
44N||3||24||Ipi caye'k we'piacimocuk Se'mwInIn ipi ki ke'naktone'wacuk e'tshowat kakItwat winwake' okinikan iactanawa notI e'kishkiwuk.
44N||3||25||KinwasI ktonicansumkowak Nakan acimocuk, ipi wawitmatwun, Kshe'mIne'to kawawitmowat kosnanIn okinan E'pIne'e'mIn, ipi knicansuk caye'k noe'twun shotI kik kIshwe'ntakwsik.
44N||3||26||Kshe'mIne'to kapsukwitnat okwIsIn CisusIn, okinokanan kinwa ne'tum e'wishwe'nmukwie'k, e'wiwe'pnumakwie'k kmiashuwe'psiwnawan.
44N||4||1||Me'kwe'cI e'ie'knonawat ni nIshInape'n me'matmoncIn ipi Kapte'n shi kcI-nume'okumkok ipi Se'cwsiuk, oki pie'naskakwan.
44N||4||2||Kikisate'ntumwuk e'ki knomowanIt ni nIshInape'n, ipi e'kie'kwe'nIt, i e'wionIshkanIt, ni ne'poncIn shi CisusIn.
44N||4||3||OkimshunawancI, ipi okikpakwawan nash wiapnInuk osam e'nmupkonianuk.
44N||4||4||NIshcI mce'sh okite'pwe'takwan, kanotakwat nianuk mtatswak nInwuk kitshik kate'pwe'takwat.
44N||4||5||KanomkukcI wiapuk kiw nakanse'cuk, ipi otukwe'simowan, ipi we'npie'makwcIn.
44N||4||6||Ipi E'ne's ke'cmatmot, ipi Ke'Ipe's ipi Can, ipi E'nukse'ntu, ipi e'tshowat e'nwe'mawacIn ni ke'cmatmonIt kimaoce'tik shi Cinose'ne'muk.
44N||4||7||IwcI na‘wiukwan kacipitupawat okinatowawan. We'kwnicI kshke'osuwun tanakI we'ni otInoswunuk otI kaocItotme'k.
44N||4||8||IwcI Pitu e'moshkIne'shkakot, PanakwsIncIn CipamIn, otI okinan, kinwa nakane'nmukwie'k nIshInape'k, ipi e'kwe'simukwie'k ki isne'iun
44N||4||9||KishpIn nkom e'kishkiwuk natakoik, we'cmnototwut, otI pwanu‘pmose't otI nInI, kaocI ne'se't?
44N||4||10||Kuke'ntanawa kinwa caye'k, ipi caye'k nIshInape'k shi isne'iuk, shiw tInoswunuk Cisus Knayst Ne'se'ni nInI kaskakowe'k Kshe'mIne'to kapsukwitnat e'kinponIt, winsI otI nInI we'cnipwIt e'ne'se't e'nasmupie'k.
44N||4||11||OtIsI ie'i sIn, kawe'pne'me'k we'ske'ie'k, iw sI ie'i ne'tmIsuk shi e'wikwe'ak.
44N||4||12||Coke' pe'kanuk ke'skonwe'wun otItosin cowi pe'kanuk noswun namiukwun kishkok minasik ninwuk ke'ocI ke'skonkoikon.
44N||4||13||IwcI kawaptumwawat i onikansiunawa ni PituIn ipi CanIn, e'ke'nmawat ke'ko e'pwake'ntumnIt okimamkate'nmawan ipi okinaktowe'nmawan e'kipmowice'wanIt ni CisusIn.
44N||4||14||Ipi e'wapmawat, ni nInwun, kane'se'mIt e'wickapwItakwat coke'ko okinasiwan.
44N||4||15||PicI kamace'nashkawawat shi e'tshI kikitowat okitshItanawa winwa.
44N||4||16||OtI kItwuk,TInicI ke'totwukon kotI nInwuk we'we'ne'se' mataonokie'wun kitotmok ke'iapI caye'k waptanawa e'tacuk shi Cinose'ne'muk, coce' ktanIiakwne'tsimIn.
